# Courtier gets a tooth extraction
VIETmisc.0121 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0121.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0121.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:scope_VIET_tooth_extracted
		animation = happiness
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_tooth_extracted
		}	
		scope:scope_VIET_tooth_extracted = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_skilled_tooth_extraction
				years = 5
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0121.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0121.info
		}
	}	
	option = { # Reward the barber
		name = VIETmisc.0121.b
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0121.info
		}
	}
}

# A new shop opens in town
VIETmisc.0124 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0124.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0124.desc
	theme = stewardship_wealth_focus
	override_background = { reference = market }
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
	}
	
	option = { # No thanks
		name = VIETmisc.0124.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # I'll take it
		name = VIETmisc.0124.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_trinkets_odds_and_ends
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # I'll buy it
		name = VIETmisc.0124.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 10
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 10
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_trinkets_odds_and_ends
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			callous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # You suck
		name = VIETmisc.0124.d
		add_dread = 8
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
			humble = medium_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

		name = VIETmisc.0127.c
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Help them out
		name = VIETmisc.0127.d
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Hire them
		name = VIETmisc.0127.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_hired_new_dutiful_servants
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}



# Come across an abandoned baby - what to do?
VIETmisc.0128 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0128.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0128.desc
	theme = family
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_skyrim_forest }
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
		animation = newborn
	}
	
	#lower_center_portrait = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			exists = house
			NOT = { is_close_or_extended_family_of = root }
			is_married = no
			is_concubine = no
			OR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
				has_trait = generous
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = wrathful
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				exists = house
				NOT = { is_close_or_extended_family_of = root }
				is_married = no
				is_concubine = no
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = just
					has_trait = generous
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = wrathful
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 1 2 }
				gender_female_chance = 50
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
				random_traits = yes
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {				
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
			}
			# scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
			# 	add_character_modifier = {
			# 		modifier = VIET_abaonded_as_a_child
			# 	}
			# }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Leave it to die
		name = VIETmisc.0128.a
		add_dread = 20
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_abandoned_a_baby
			years = 10
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_abandoned_baby
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_gain
				compassionate = massive_stress_impact_gain
				just = medium_stress_impact_gain
				generous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_wolves # Maybe something else in the future?
				}			
			}
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_rival_reason_placeholder
		}
	}		
	option = { # Let a servant adopt it
		name = VIETmisc.0128.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_saved_abandoned_baby
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = major_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { # Let courtier adopt it
		name = VIETmisc.0128.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_saved_abandoned_baby
			years = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				set_mother = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer		
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
					is_female = no
				}
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				set_father = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer		
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#We take care of the sundries in a hidden effect so as not to put too much into the tooltip.
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = { set_house = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer.house }
			add_courtier = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
			scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
				add_opinion = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
					modifier = VIET_opinion_adopted_child
				}	
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
					modifier = VIET_opinion_adopted_parent
				}	
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = major_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
	}	
}

# Otumeel - Prankster who breaks in people's not to steal, but to move things around
VIETmisc.0129 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0129.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0129.desc
	theme = prison
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster
		animation = schadenfreude
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 18 30 }
				gender_female_chance = 0
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster
				random_traits = no
				trait = education_intrigue_3
				trait = gregarious
				trait = arbitrary
				trait = content				
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster = {
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_otumeel_prankster
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Don't do it again
		name = VIETmisc.0129.a
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}			
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # Pay a fine
		name = VIETmisc.0129.b
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # Stay in prison!
		name = VIETmisc.0129.c
		add_dread = 5
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = medium_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = medium_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			content = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # You look handy
		name = VIETmisc.0129.d
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		add_courtier = scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster
					type = loyalty_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_otumeel_prankster
				type = loyalty_hook
			}
		}
	}	
}

	}

# Meet a little brother and sister
VIETmisc.0133 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0133.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0133.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	override_icon = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_family.dds"
	}
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Good kid
		name = VIETmisc.0133.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = compassionate
			}
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}			
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
				wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
				callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}		
		}
	}		
	option = { # Play with kids
		name = VIETmisc.0133.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				NOT = {
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}			
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
				wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
				callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}		
		}
	}		
	option = { # Tell them to scram
		name = VIETmisc.0133.c
		add_dread = 10
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}	
	option = { # Push them off the bridge into river
		name = VIETmisc.0133.d
		add_dread = 10
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = compassionate
				}
				OR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = vengeful
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				callous = minor_stress_impact_loss
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_loss
				wrathful = minor_stress_impact_loss
				vengeful = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}			
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				forgiving = medium_stress_impact_gain
				compassionate = major_stress_impact_gain
				patient = medium_stress_impact_gain
				calm = medium_stress_impact_gain
			}	
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				# Didn't hurt kids, no one saw
				10 = {
					send_interface_toast = {
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0133.toast.1
					}
				}
				# Didn't hurt kids, people saw
				10 = {
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0133.toast.2
						VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
					}
				}
				# Hurt kids, no one saw
				10 = {
					send_interface_toast = {
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0133.toast.3
						add_character_modifier = {
							modifier = VIET_hurt_kids_no_witness
							years = 7					
						}
					}
				}
				# Hurt kids, people saw
				10 = {
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0133.toast.4
						VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
						add_character_modifier = {
							modifier = VIET_hurt_kids_witnesses
							years = 7						
						}
					}
				}
			}		
		}
	}	
}

# A courtier is feeling sad today
VIETmisc.0135 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0135.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0135.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:scope_VIET_sad_person
		animation = sadness
	}	
	right_portrait = root	

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_sad_person
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Comfort
		name = VIETmisc.0135.a
		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_sad_person = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_comforted_me
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_sad_person
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}		
	option = { # Leave
		name = VIETmisc.0135.b
	}			
	option = { # Mock them
		name = VIETmisc.0135.c
		VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_sad_person = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_mocked_me
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_sad_person
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_rival_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
}

# Character comes across a run-down orphanage
VIETmisc.0138 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0138.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0138.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	override_icon = { reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_family.dds" }
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Oh well
		name = VIETmisc.0138.a
	}	
	option = { # Donate
		name = VIETmisc.0138.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 20
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = generous
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
				generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
				callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
				cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
				paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Donate a lot
		name = VIETmisc.0138.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 40
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 40
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = generous
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
				generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
				callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
				cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
				paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}		
		}
	}
	option = { # Be jaded
		name = VIETmisc.0138.d
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_jaded_about_charity
			years = 8
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}




# Courtier is friends with a beggar
VIETmisc.0139 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0139.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0139.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = scope:scope_VIET_beggar_friend

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes # Someone who is nice
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes # Someone who is nice			
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_beggar_friend
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_beggar_friend
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I see
		name = VIETmisc.0139.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Bad
		name = VIETmisc.0139.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_beggar_friend = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_judgmental
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Hire him
		name = VIETmisc.0139.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 10
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 10
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_hired_beggar_servant
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}


# Courtier trips and is helped by another
VIETmisc.0140 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0140.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0140.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	
	left_portrait = scope:scope_VIET_helper
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_tripper
		animation = severelywounded
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes # Someone who is nice
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes # Someone who is nice			
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_helper
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_tripper
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_helper
				modifier = VIET_opinion_helped_me_when_i_tripped
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = { # help
		name = VIETmisc.0140.a
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_tripper = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_helped_me_when_i_tripped
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # nbd
		name = VIETmisc.0140.b
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_tripper = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disregarded_injury
			}			
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:scope_VIET_tripper
					title = VIETmisc.0140.toast
					scope:scope_VIET_tripper = {
						increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = fall }
					}
				}
			}		
		}
	}
}

		}

	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Here are some funds
		name = VIETmisc.0147.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 15
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_almshouse_donation
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Here are a lot of funds
		name = VIETmisc.0147.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 40
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 40
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_almshouse_donation
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			callous = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # No
		name = VIETmisc.0147.c
		stress_impact = {
			generous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

		animation = personality_honorable
	}

		base = 1

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	
	option = { # You keep it
		name = VIETmisc.0156.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_massive_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_humble_generosity
			years = 10
		}
	}	
	option = { # Split it between the two of you
		name = VIETmisc.0156.b
		add_gold = 50
	}	
	option = { # I keep it!
		name = VIETmisc.0156.c
		add_gold = 100
		add_dread = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_massive_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Horny courtier talks about a harlot he had sex with
VIETmisc.0157 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0157.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0157.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disgust
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:horny
		animation = schadenfreude
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			is_married = no
			is_female = no
			NOR = {
				has_sexuality = asexual
				has_sexuality = homosexual
				has_trait = chaste
				has_trait = celibate
				is_eunuch_trigger = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_trait = lustful
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = arbitrary
				has_trait = lazy
				has_trait = gluttonous
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				is_married = no
				is_female = no
				NOR = {
					has_sexuality = asexual
					has_sexuality = homosexual
					has_trait = chaste
					has_trait = celibate
					is_eunuch_trigger = yes
				}
				OR = {
					has_trait = lustful
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = lazy
					has_trait = gluttonous
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_100_love_techniques
				years = 10
			}
			save_scope_as = horny
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Steer it to another topic
		name = VIETmisc.0157.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = lustful
						trait_is_virtue = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = lustful
						trait_is_sin = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lustful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Call the guy out on it
		name = VIETmisc.0157.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = lustful
						trait_is_virtue = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = lustful
						trait_is_sin = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:horny = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_techniques_prude
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lustful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Learn more about it
		name = VIETmisc.0157.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = lustful
						trait_is_virtue = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = lustful
						trait_is_sin = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_100_love_techniques
			years = 10
		}
		scope:horny = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_techniques_agreement
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = medium_stress_impact_gain
			celibate = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

	}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Not my problem
		name = VIETmisc.0159.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_refused_cat_lady_issue
			years = 10
		}

		}
	}

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_did_something_cat_lady_issue
			years = 10
		}

			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Imprison lady, kill her cats
		name = VIETmisc.0159.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		trait = sadistic
		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_dread = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_did_something_cat_lady_issue
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			humble = medium_stress_impact_gain
			patient = minor_stress_impact_gain
			calm = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Imprison lady, kill her cats
		name = VIETmisc.0159.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = callous
			NOT = {
				has_trait = sadistic
			}
		}
		trait = callous
		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_dread = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_did_something_cat_lady_issue
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			humble = medium_stress_impact_gain

			calm = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

# Spouse has over a hundred fancy shoes
VIETmisc.0161 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0161.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0161.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:spouse
		animation = shame
	}
	
	trigger = {
		is_married = yes
		any_spouse = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = greedy
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = lazy
				has_trait = arbitrary
				has_trait = ambitious
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = content
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = generous
			}
			is_ruler = no
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = greedy
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = lazy
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = ambitious
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = humble
					has_trait = generous
				}
				is_ruler = no
			}	
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_owns_a_lot_of_shoes
				years = 10
			}	
			save_scope_as = spouse
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Sell it off
		name = VIETmisc.0161.a
		scope:spouse = {
			remove_character_modifier = VIET_owns_a_lot_of_shoes
			add_gold = 50
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_sell_shoes
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Not my problem
		name = VIETmisc.0161.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Until The Night Turns - courtier dreams about the end of the world and enjoys it
# https://youtu.be/fR821cKklVU
VIETmisc.0166 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0166.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0166.desc
	theme = friendly
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:world_ender
		animation = personality_content
	}	
	

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			has_trait_extroverted_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				has_trait_extroverted_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = world_ender
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_hedonistic_apocalypse
				years = 4
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Hedonism bad
		name = VIETmisc.0166.a
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes	
		scope:world_ender = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disapproves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Hedonism good
		name = VIETmisc.0166.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes	
		scope:world_ender = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_approves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}



# Dead Man's Hand - ghost appears in a dream asking not to be buried
# https://youtu.be/tdP2z4juRHg
VIETmisc.0167 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0167.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0167.desc
	theme = VIET_lord_huron_strange_trails
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:dead_man
		animation = beg
	}	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = paranoia
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			location = root.capital_province
			age = { 20 60 }
			gender = male
			faith = root.faith
			culture = root.culture
			dynasty = none
			random_traits = yes
			save_scope_as = dead_man
			trait = maimed
			trait = wounded_3
		}
		scope:dead_man = {
			VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes		
			death = {
				death_reason = death_attacked
			}
		}	
	}

	
	option = { # Help un-bury
		name = VIETmisc.0167.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0167.a.toast
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_wandering_ghost_blessing
						years = 6
					}
				}				
			}	
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Keep buried
		name = VIETmisc.0167.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0167.b.toast
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_wandering_ghost_nightmares
						years = 6
					}
				}				
			}	
		}
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

# Fool for Love (my favorite Lord Huron song!) - meet the Fool for Love by the side of the road
# https://youtu.be/uLxIYSNoZvw
VIETmisc.0170 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0170.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0170.desc
	theme = VIET_lord_huron_strange_trails
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:dreamer
		animation = personality_compassionate
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:fool_for_love
		animation = severelywounded
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		num_sinful_traits < 1
		NOR = {
			has_trait = callous
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
	}
	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.3
			num_virtuous_traits > 1
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.3
			num_virtuous_traits < 1
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer } }		
			add_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
		}
		# Choose whether to meet the male or female Dreamer
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male } }
					set_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					change_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
						add = 1
					}		
				}
				character:VIET_character_001 = {
					save_scope_as = dreamer
				}
			}
			10 = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female } }
					set_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					change_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
						add = 1
					}		
				}
				character:VIET_character_002 = {
					save_scope_as = dreamer
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 20 35 }
				gender_female_chance = 0
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = fool_for_love
				random_traits = yes
				#random_traits_list = {
				#	count = 3
				#	ambitious = {}
				#	arrogant = {}
				#	lustful = {}
				#	brave = {}
				#	diligent = {}
				#	wrathful = {}
				#	trusting = {}
				#	impatient = {}
				#	gregarious = {}
				#}
				#trait = maimed
				trait = wounded_2
			}
			scope:fool_for_love = {	
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes	
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}
			}			
		}
	}

	
	option = { # I am a fool for love
		name = VIETmisc.0170.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_yang_wisdom } }
			set_variable = {
				name = VIET_dreamer_yang_wisdom
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = VIET_dreamer_yang_wisdom
				add = 1
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # I am not a fool for love
		name = VIETmisc.0170.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_yin_wisdom } }
			set_variable = {
				name = VIET_dreamer_yin_wisdom
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = VIET_dreamer_yin_wisdom
				add = 1
			}		
		}		
	}	
	option = { # The Dreamer???
		name = VIETmisc.0170.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_yang_wisdom } }
					set_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_yang_wisdom
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					change_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_yang_wisdom
						add = 1
					}		
				}
			}
			10 = {
				VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { exists = var:VIET_dreamer_yin_wisdom } }
					set_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_yin_wisdom
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					change_variable = {
						name = VIET_dreamer_yin_wisdom
						add = 1
					}		
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = VIETmisc.0177
			months = { 12 96 }
		}	
	}
	
}

	}

						modifier = VIET_meet_me_in_the_woods

			}

	}

# Cursed - courtier claims to be cursed by a courtesan but seems to be obsessed with her more than anything
# https://youtu.be/UbSsLPBw9l8
VIETmisc.0175 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0175.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0175.desc
	theme = intrigue_temptation_focus
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }
	
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:horny
		animation = personality_vengeful
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait_extroverted_trigger = yes
				has_trait_malicious_trigger = yes
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = arrogant
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes
				has_trait = humble
			}	
			is_female = no
			is_married = no
			num_of_relation_lover < 1
			NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
			NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
		}	
	}
	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait_extroverted_trigger = yes
					has_trait_malicious_trigger = yes
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes
					has_trait = humble
				}	
				is_female = no
				is_married = no
				num_of_relation_lover < 1
				NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
				NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_obsessed_with_a_courtesan
				years = 6
			}
			save_scope_as = horny
		}
	}
	
	option = { # naughty naughty
		name = VIETmisc.0175.a		
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = chaste
						trait_is_virtue = lustful
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = lustful
						trait_is_virtue = chaste
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {		
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain		
			lustful = minor_stress_impact_gain		
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
		}	
		scope:horny = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shamed_courtesan
			}			
		}
	}	
	option = { # don't go crazy
		name = VIETmisc.0175.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {		
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
		}	
		scope:horny = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shamed_courtesan
			}			
		}
	}	
	option = { # What bad stuff did you do?
		name = VIETmisc.0175.c
		trigger = {
			can_add_hook = {
				type = threat_hook
				target = scope:horny
			}
		}
		add_hook = {
			type = threat_hook
			target = scope:horny
			years = 5
		}
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {		
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
		}	
		scope:horny = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_suspects_terrible_things
			}			
		}
	}	
	option = { # I'm horny
		name = VIETmisc.0175.d
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_eunuch_trigger = yes
				has_trait = celibate
				has_sexuality = asexual
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					OR = {
						has_sexuality = homosexual						
						has_sexuality = bisexual						
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lustful_ruler
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {		
			chaste = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		scope:horny = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_wants_my_courtesan
			}			
		}
	}
}





# Way Out There - meet a crazy old man talking about the Dreamers and strange trails
# https://youtu.be/gAbqaW_xLlQ
VIETmisc.0176 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0176.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0176.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worried
	}	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
				add = 1
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
				add = 1
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0176.a
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
			}
		}
		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0176.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
			}
		}
		VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0176.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_male
				exists = var:VIET_dreamer_karmic_connection_female
			}
		}
		VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
	}
}

# Night We Met - courtier wishes he could have done something to save a dead lover
# https://youtu.be/nG0HrAVIw_c
VIETmisc.0178 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0178.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0178.desc
	theme = death	
	override_background = { reference = garden }
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:sad_guy
		animation = grief
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}
	

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait_extroverted_trigger = yes
				has_trait_malicious_trigger = yes
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = arrogant
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes
				has_trait = humble
			}	
			is_female = no
			is_married = no
			num_of_relation_lover < 1
			NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
			NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
		}	
	}
	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		#play_music_cue = mx_cue_touching_moment
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait_extroverted_trigger = yes
					has_trait_malicious_trigger = yes
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait_benevolent_trigger = yes
					has_trait = humble
				}	
				is_female = no
				is_married = no
				num_of_relation_lover < 1
				NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
				NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_night_we_met
				years = 8
			}
			save_scope_as = sad_guy
		}
	}

	
	option = { # stop obsessing about trying to change the past
		name = VIETmisc.0178.a
		random_list = {
			10 = { VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
		stress_impact = {		
			deceitful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:sad_guy = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_moving_on_advice
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # she's in a better place
		name = VIETmisc.0178.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {		
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		scope:sad_guy = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_moving_on_advice
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # stop being whiny
		name = VIETmisc.0178.c
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {		
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain	
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		scope:sad_guy = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_moving_on_advice
			}		
		}
	}
}

# Courtier has crappy handwriting
VIETmisc.0180 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0180.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0180.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus

	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:bad_handwriting	
		animation = chancellor	
	}	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}	
	

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			# Want someone who's probably literate
			NOT = { has_trait = blind }
			probably_unintelligent_trigger = no
			OR = {
				probably_intelligent_trigger = yes
				diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
		}
		# Weed out most cultures that probably aren't literate at the game start and wouldn't be writing stuff like letters
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				# Want someone who's probably literate
				NOT = { has_trait = blind }
				probably_unintelligent_trigger = no
				OR = {
					probably_intelligent_trigger = yes
					diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = bad_handwriting
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_horrible_handwriting }
				}
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_horrible_handwriting
				}
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Mock them
		name = VIETmisc.0180.a
		scope:bad_handwriting = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_mocked_handwriting
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_trait = compassionate }
			}
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_loss
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_loss
				arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = compassionate
			}
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
				humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # Tease them
		name = VIETmisc.0180.b
		duel = {
			skill = diplomacy
			target = scope:bad_handwriting
			10 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -1.1
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0180.tease_toast_bad
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:bad_handwriting
					title = VIETmisc.0180.tease_toast_bad
					scope:bad_handwriting = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_tease_handwriting_bad
						}
					}
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 1.1
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0180.tease_toast_good
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:bad_handwriting
					title = VIETmisc.0180.tease_toast_good
					scope:bad_handwriting = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_tease_handwriting_good
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Make no comment
		name = VIETmisc.0180.c
		stress_impact = {
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Give them advice
		name = VIETmisc.0180.d
		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = learning
		scope:bad_handwriting = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_constructive_criticism_handwriting
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		random = {
			chance = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				has_trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				has_trait = impatient
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				has_trait = calm
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				has_trait = wrathful
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				has_trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				has_trait = lazy
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				learning <= low_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				learning >= medium_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				learning <= mediocre_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				stewardship >= decent_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				stewardship <= low_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				stewardship >= medium_skill_rating
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -2
				stewardship <= mediocre_skill_rating
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0180.tease_toast_great
			send_interface_toast = {
				type = event_toast_effect_good
				left_icon = scope:bad_handwriting
				title = VIETmisc.0180.tease_toast_great
				scope:bad_handwriting = {
					remove_character_modifier = VIET_horrible_handwriting
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}




# Writing too much makes your wrists sore
VIETmisc.0181 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0181.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0181.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = sadness
	}	

	trigger = {
		# Weed out most cultures that probably aren't literate at the game start and wouldn't be writing stuff like letters
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Stop writing
		name = VIETmisc.0181.a
		VIET_random_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Keep writing!
		name = VIETmisc.0181.b
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_wrists_hurt
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

			has_trait = trusting

	}

	}

		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}

	
	option = { # so weird
		name = VIETmisc.0185.a
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_food_chat
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_food_chat
			}			
		}
	}
}

# Spooked by a frogmouth bird

	type = character_event

	desc = VIETmisc.0196.desc
	theme = travel_danger

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = fear
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		is_location_valid_for_travel_event_on_land = yes
		location = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_india
				geographical_region = world_burma
				geographical_region = world_asia_southeast
				geographical_region = custom_viet_lands
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0196.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_by_animal
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {		
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0196.info
		}
	}	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0196.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_avoiding_strange_creatures
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {		
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0196.info
		}
	}
}


# Camels killed by karakurt spiders

	type = character_event

	desc = VIETmisc.0197.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = courtyard }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = ghw_region_transoxiana
				geographical_region = ghw_region_siberia
				geographical_region = special_mongol_empire_chagatai_region
			}
		}		
	}

		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {

			has_trait = brave
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok

		}

			is_landless_type_title = no

				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
					geographical_region = world_europe
					geographical_region = world_africa_north
					geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
					geographical_region = world_asia_korea
					geographical_region = world_asia_china
					geographical_region = world_asia_japan
					geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
					geographical_region = world_asia_sakhalin_hokkaido

				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier

				years = 5
			}
		}

		if = {

				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on

		}

}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}

		}

# Scared by the red eyes of an apollo butterfly
VIETmisc.0205 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0205.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0205.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = fear
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = schadenfreude
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = calm
				has_trait = content
				has_trait = patient
				has_trait = trusting
				probably_intelligent_trigger = yes
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
			NOT = { has_trait = craven }
		}
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = custom_outremer
				geographical_region = world_steppe
				geographical_region = world_siberia
				geographical_region = world_tibet
				geographical_region = world_asia_china
				geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
			}
			NOT = { geographical_region = world_europe_west_britannia }
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_stress 
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = calm
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = patient
					has_trait = trusting
					probably_intelligent_trigger = yes
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = craven }
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0205.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {		
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			honest = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0205.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0205.b
		stress_impact = {		
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0205.info
		}
	}

				geographical_region = world_asia_indonesia
				geographical_region = custom_viet_lands
				geographical_region = tgp_yue_region
				geographical_region = tgp_dian_region
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0207.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { # Turns out to be a deer
					show_chance = no
					desc = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_not_a_tiger
					custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_not_a_tiger_name
				}
				50 = { # Tiger attacks you
					show_chance = no
					desc = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_a_tiger
					custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_a_tiger_name
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { # Tiger attacks you
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_a_tiger
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_a_tiger_desc
						random = {
							chance = 33
							increase_wounds_effect = { REASON = accident }
						}
						stress_impact = {		
							base = medium_stress_impact_gain
							craven = medium_stress_impact_gain
						}
					}
				}
				50 = { # Turns out to be a deer
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_good
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_not_a_tiger
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0207.toast.its_not_a_tiger_desc
						VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
					}
				}		
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {		
			craven = medium_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0207.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0207.b
		stress_impact = {		
			brave = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_loss
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0207.info
		}
	}

}



# Hyrax is chilling on the rocks
VIETmisc.0208 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0208.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0208.desc
	theme = travel_intrigue
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_skyrim_forest }
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:hyrax_watcher
		animation = disapproval
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		is_location_valid_for_travel_event_on_land = yes
		current_travel_plan = {
			any_entourage_character = {	
				is_available_travelling = yes
			}
		}
		location = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_africa_sahara
				geographical_region = world_africa_west
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = ghw_region_egypt
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_arabia
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		current_travel_plan = {
			random_entourage_character = {
				limit = {
					is_available_travelling = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = hyrax_watcher
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0208.a
		VIET_tiny_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0208.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0208.b
		VIET_tiny_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0208.info
		}
	}

}

# Honey badger don't care - it killed a lot of chickens belonging to a farmer
VIETmisc.0210 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0210.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0210.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	left_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			is_landless_type_title = no
			any_county_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_africa_sahara
					geographical_region = custom_sahara_proper
					geographical_region = world_africa_west
					geographical_region = world_africa_east
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_arabia
					geographical_region = ghw_region_persia
					geographical_region = world_transoxiana
					geographical_region = world_india
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0210.a
		stress_impact = {
			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0210.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0210.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0210.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0210.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_charitable_to_struggling_peasant
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0210.info
		}
	}

}

# Solve sparrow problem by setting up sparrow traps at home to catch them for their meat?
VIETmisc.0214 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0214.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0214.desc
	theme = stewardship_domain_focus
	override_icon = { reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_feast.dds" } 
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:sparrow_eater
		animation = personality_content
	}
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = gluttonous
				has_trait = diligent
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = generous
			}
		}
		capital_province = {
			NOR = { # Places with no house sparrows
				geographical_region = world_africa_west
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = world_tibet
				geographical_region = world_asia_china
				geographical_region = world_asia_korea
				geographical_region = world_asia_japan
				geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_sakhalin_hokkaido
				geographical_region = world_asia_southeast_islands
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = gluttonous
					has_trait = diligent
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = generous
				}
			}
			# add_character_modifier = {
			# 	modifier = VIET_eating_sparrow
			# 	years = 8
			# }
			save_scope_as = sparrow_eater
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0214.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			gluttonous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:sparrow_eater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disapproves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0214.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0214.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_sparrow
			years = 8
		}
		scope:sparrow_eater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_approves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0214.info
		}
	}

}
