					geographical_region = world_steppe
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_siberia
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = gluttonous
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = lustful
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = trusting
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = paranoid }
				NOT = { has_trait = temperate }
				NOT = { religion = religion:jainism_religion }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_coturnism
				years = 2
			}
			save_scope_as = quail_eater
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0215.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:quail_eater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_sympathy_coturnism
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0215.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0215.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		duel = {
			skill = diplomacy
			target = scope:quail_eater
			10 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -1.1
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:quail_eater
					title = VIETmisc.0215.b.tooltip.bad
					scope:quail_eater = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_lecture_coturnism_bad
						}
					}
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 1.1
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:quail_eater
					title = VIETmisc.0215.b.tooltip.good
					scope:quail_eater = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_lecture_coturnism_good
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0215.info
		}
	}
}



# Encounter black winged stilts by some ponds
VIETmisc.0216 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0216.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0216.desc
	theme = travel_stewardship
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_skyrim_forest } 
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		is_location_valid_for_travel_event_on_land = yes
		location = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_west
				geographical_region = world_europe_west_francia
				geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia
				geographical_region = world_europe_south
				geographical_region = world_middle_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = world_india
				geographical_region = world_burma
				geographical_region = world_siberia
				geographical_region = world_asia
				geographical_region = world_tibet
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0216.a
		trigger = {
			learning < decent_skill_rating	
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0216.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0216.b
		trigger = {
			learning < decent_skill_rating	
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_learning_about_birds
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0216.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0216.c
		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = learning
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_impressed_others_animal_knowledge
			years = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0216.info
		}
	}
}




# Noble wants to hunt nilgai that is sacred to a village
VIETmisc.0217 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0217.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0217.desc
	theme = hunt_activity
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			is_landless_type_title = no
			any_county_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_burma
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0217.a
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0217.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0217.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_let_noble_hunt_nilgai
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0217.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0217.c
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_protected_sacred_nilgai
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0217.info
		}
	}
}

# Servant sees a parliament of rooks in your garden
VIETmisc.0221 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0221.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0221.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = garden }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = custom_outremer
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_steppe
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = world_siberia
				geographical_region = world_asia_china
				geographical_region = world_asia_korea
				geographical_region = world_asia_north_east
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0221.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0221.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0221.b
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 40
				modifier = {
					add = 15
					num_sinful_traits >= 1
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -15				
					num_virtuous_traits >= 1
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0221.b.tooltip
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_rook_curse
						years = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0221.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0221.c
		trigger = {
			VIET_is_crow_lord_or_lady_trigger = yes
		}
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_befriending_rooks
			years = 8
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0221.info
		}
	}
}

				geographical_region = custom_burgundy
				geographical_region = world_europe_south_italy
				geographical_region = custom_bavaria
				geographical_region = custom_core_switzerland
				geographical_region = world_europe_south_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = custom_hungary
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	option = { # buy the meat
		name = VIETmisc.0224.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 15
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_chamois
			years = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
	option = { # threaten the hunters to give you the meat
		name = VIETmisc.0224.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = greedy
						trait_is_sin = callous
						trait_is_sin = sadistic
						trait_is_sin = arbitrary
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_massive_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 10
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_chamois
			years = 3
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_threatened_hunters
			years = 6
		}
		stress_impact = {
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Ok cool story bro
		name = VIETmisc.0224.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Share hunting tips
		name = VIETmisc.0224.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = lifestyle_hunter
		}
		#trait = lifestyle_hunter
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			15 = { add_martial_skill = 1 }
			15 = { add_prowess_skill = 1 }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
}


# Town notable invites you to participate in caracal pigeon hunting blood sport gambling
VIETmisc.0225 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0225.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0225.desc
	theme = hunt_activity
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			is_landless_type_title = no
			any_county_province = {
				OR = { # Mainly seems to be a India/Central Asian phenomenon
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
				}		
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # observe
		name = VIETmisc.0225.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0225.info
		}
	}
	option = { # bet on the winner
		name = VIETmisc.0225.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0225.toast.good
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0225.toast.good
					random_list = {
						40 = { add_gold = 15 }
						30 = { add_gold = 25 }
						20 = { add_gold = 35 }
						10 = { add_gold = 45 }
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue <= low_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue <= mediocre_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial <= low_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial <= mediocre_skill_rating
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0225.toast.bad
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0225.toast.bad
					stress_impact = {
						base = minor_stress_impact_gain
						greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
						wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
					}
					random_list = {
						40 = { remove_short_term_gold = 15 }
						30 = { remove_short_term_gold = 25 }
						20 = { remove_short_term_gold = 35 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 45 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0225.info
		}
	}
	option = { # have other business to take care of
		name = VIETmisc.0225.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0225.info
		}
	}
}



# Heard some yellowhammer songbird singing
VIETmisc.0226 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0226.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0226.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = happiness
	}
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			is_landless_type_title = no
			any_county_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_europe
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
					geographical_region = ghw_region_holy_land
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_steppe_west
					geographical_region = world_steppe_east
					geographical_region = world_steppe_central
					geographical_region = world_siberia
				}		
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0226.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0226.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0226.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_listened_to_yellowhammer
			years = 4
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_listened_to_yellowhammer
				years = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0226.info
		}
	}
}

# Pig is put on trial for the murder of a child

	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0229.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0229.desc
	theme = intrigue_skulduggery_focus
	override_background = { reference = gallows }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_vengeful
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events }
			culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
		}
		# Weed out cultures that wouldn't have these kinds of legal proceedings
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
		# Wouldn't make sense for these religions
		NOR = { 
			religion = religion:islam_religion
			religion = religion:judaism_religion
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_murder
	}

	option = { # ok

		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes

			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on

		}
	}
}




# Butcher is giving up trade to become a wandering preacher and care for animals
VIETmisc.0230 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0230.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0230.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	trigger = {
		# Pick religions for which it would make sense
		OR = {
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_abrahamic }
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_eastern }
			faith = {
				OR = {
					has_doctrine = tenet_dharmic_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_reincarnation
					trait_is_sin = gluttonous
					trait_is_sin = sadistic
					trait_is_sin = callous
					trait_is_sin = wrathful
					trait_is_virtue = compassionate
					trait_is_virtue = temperate
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = gruesome_festivals_active } }
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = human_sacrifice_active } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0230.a
		stress_impact = {
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0230.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0230.c
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

				OR = {
					has_doctrine = tenet_dharmic_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_mendicant_preachers
					has_doctrine = tenet_monasticism
					has_doctrine = tenet_asceticism
					has_doctrine = tenet_sanctity_of_nature
					trait_is_sin = sadistic
					trait_is_sin = callous
					trait_is_virtue = compassionate
					trait_is_virtue = generous
					trait_is_virtue = humble
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = gruesome_festivals_active } }
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = human_sacrifice_active } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0232.a
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0232.b
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0232.c
		VIET_massive_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_listened_to_saint_francis
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

		}

			days = 1453
		}
	}

		modifier = {
			add = 0.2

		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	
	option = { # It's okay, I don't mind

		}	
	}

		name = VIETmisc.0235.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Help her buy clothes
		name = VIETmisc.0235.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = generous
		}
		trait = generous
		remove_short_term_gold = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_charity_to_servant
			years = 4
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}

}

# Prisoner is on friendly terms with guards and is a regular who gets imprisoned a lot for silly reasons
VIETmisc.0237 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0237.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0237.desc
	theme = prison
	override_icon = { reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_relation_friendly.dds" } 
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:spunky
		animation = happiness
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 18 30 }
				gender_female_chance = 100
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = spunky
				random_traits = no
				#trait = education_diplomacy_3
				trait = gregarious
				trait = just
				trait = brave				
				trait = honest			
			}
			scope:spunky = {
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_spunky_girl
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = { add_trait = education_diplomacy_1 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_diplomacy_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_diplomacy_3 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_stewardship_1 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_stewardship_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_stewardship_3 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_intrigue_1 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_intrigue_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_intrigue_3 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_learning_1 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_learning_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = education_learning_3 }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { }
					30 = { add_trait = intellect_good_1 }
					20 = { add_trait = intellect_good_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = intellect_good_3 }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { }
					30 = { add_trait = beauty_good_1 }
					20 = { add_trait = beauty_good_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = beauty_good_3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0237.a
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:spunky = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0237.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:spunky = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0237.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_courtier = scope:spunky
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:spunky
					type = loyalty_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:spunky
				type = loyalty_hook
			}
		}
	}
}

# Discussion about whether it is better to be a master of something or a jack of all trades
VIETmisc.0239 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0239.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0239.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = garden }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:generalist
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:specialist
		animation = disapproval
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = stubborn
				has_trait = ambitious
				has_trait = impatient
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = stubborn
				has_trait = ambitious
				has_trait = impatient
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = ambitious
					has_trait = impatient
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = specialist
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = ambitious
					has_trait = impatient
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = generalist
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Master one thing
		name = VIETmisc.0239.a
		scope:specialist = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shares_my_opinions
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shares_my_opinions
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Jack of all trades
		name = VIETmisc.0239.b
		scope:generalist = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shares_my_opinions
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shares_my_opinions
			}			
		}
	}
}

# A maidservant got rejected hard
VIETmisc.0241 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0241.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0241.desc
	theme = seduction
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Reassure the maid
		name = VIETmisc.0241.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_comforted_servant
			years = 4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate					
						trait_is_virtue = just				
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Who cares
		name = VIETmisc.0241.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Be a dick
		name = VIETmisc.0241.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_heartless_towards_servants
			years = 4
		}
		add_dread = 8
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = honest
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = compassionate }
			}
			stress_impact = {
				callous = minor_stress_impact_loss
				sadistic = minor_stress_impact_loss
				honest = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
				humble = medium_stress_impact_gain
				just = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Find that servant boy and give him a talking to
		name = VIETmisc.0241.d
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_defended_servants_honor
			years = 4
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate					
						trait_is_virtue = just				
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			craven = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Two courtiers debate the merit of staying positive
VIETmisc.0243 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0243.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0243.desc
	theme = friendly
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:optimist
		animation = personality_compassionate
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:realist
		animation = disapproval
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = cynical
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = depressed_1
				has_trait = depressed_genetic
			}
		}
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = cynical
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = depressed_1
				has_trait = depressed_genetic
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = cynical
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = depressed_1
					has_trait = depressed_genetic
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = realist
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = cynical
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = depressed_1
					has_trait = depressed_genetic
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = optimist
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Be optimistic
		name = VIETmisc.0243.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_positive_mindset
			years = 5
		}
		scope:optimist = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_approves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		scope:realist = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disapproves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = medium_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			depressed_1 = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			depressed_genetic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Be realist
		name = VIETmisc.0243.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_realist_mindset
			years = 5
		}
		scope:realist = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_approves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		scope:optimist = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disapproves_viewpoint
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}



# You meet a cheerful beggar who's content with her predicament
VIETmisc.0244 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0244.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0244.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Here's some money
		name = VIETmisc.0244.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 3
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 3
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate					
						trait_is_virtue = generous				
						trait_is_virtue = just				
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
			generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Cool story sis
		name = VIETmisc.0244.b
	}
	option = { # Your cheerfulness is annoying
		name = VIETmisc.0244.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate					
						trait_is_virtue = generous				
						trait_is_virtue = just				
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}



# You see a guard give a street urchin some candy and food
VIETmisc.0245 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0245.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0245.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Hopefully she'll be okay
		name = VIETmisc.0245.a
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Stop caring about them
		name = VIETmisc.0245.b
		add_dread = 5
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Help the guard adopt her
		name = VIETmisc.0245.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_benevolently_intervened_locals
			years = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate					
						trait_is_virtue = generous				
						trait_is_virtue = just				
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = compassionate }
			}
			stress_impact = {
				callous = medium_stress_impact_gain
				sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
				arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				compassionate = minor_stress_impact_loss
				humble = minor_stress_impact_loss
				just = minor_stress_impact_loss
				generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
	}
}

# Courtier praises you, which sounds suspicious
VIETmisc.0247 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0247.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0247.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	override_icon = { reference = "gfx/interface/icons/event_types/type_relation_friendly.dds" } 
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:praiser
		animation = personality_forgiving
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { has_trait = shy }
			opinion = {
				target = root
				value > -30
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = shy }
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value > -30
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = praiser
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Uh... thanks?
		name = VIETmisc.0247.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_encouraged_by_others
			years = 5
		}
		scope:praiser = {
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_encouragement
			}		
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Very sus
		name = VIETmisc.0247.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_suspicious_of_praise
			years = 5
		}
		scope:praiser = {
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_suspects_ulterior_motives
			}		
		}
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Be awkward
		name = VIETmisc.0247.c
		scope:praiser = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_awkward_silence
			}		
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_awkward_silence
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = shy
			}
			stress_impact = {
				shy = minor_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				gregarious = minor_stress_impact_gain
				trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
	}

}

# Struggling to stay awake at a council meeting
VIETmisc.0249 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0249.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0249.desc
	theme = stewardship_duty_focus
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:councilor
		animation = throne_room_conversation_2
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}

	trigger = {
		# OR = {
		# 	exists = cp:councillor_chancellor
		# 	exists = cp:councillor_marshal
		# 	exists = cp:councillor_steward
		# 	exists = cp:councillor_spymaster
		# }
		any_councillor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_councillor = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = councilor
		}	
	}

	
	option = { # Get a nap in
		name = VIETmisc.0249.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = ambitious
					has_trait = diligent
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
				ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		scope:councilor = {
			VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				opinion = -10
				modifier = insulted_opinion
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Try to stay awake
		name = VIETmisc.0249.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}

			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = gluttonous
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = zealous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = struggle_lover
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = gluttonous
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = zealous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = struggle_hater
		}
		scope:struggle_hater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:struggle_lover
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = scope:struggle_lover
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Struggles are good
		name = VIETmisc.0251.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:struggle_lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_agree
			}			
		}
		scope:struggle_hater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Struggles are bad
		name = VIETmisc.0251.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:struggle_lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
		scope:struggle_hater = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_agree
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Both good points
		name = VIETmisc.0251.c
	}

}


# Two courtiers debate if struggling for love is good
VIETmisc.0252 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0252.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0252.desc
	theme = love
	override_background = { reference = feast }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:lover
		animation = personality_greedy
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:cynic
		animation = disapproval
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
			OR = {
				has_trait = trusting
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = zealous
			}
			NOT = {
				has_trait = cynical
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = trusting
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
				OR = {
					has_trait = trusting
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = zealous
				}
				NOT = {
					has_trait = cynical
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lover
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_thinks_love_is_struggle
				years = 5
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = trusting
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = zealous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = cynic
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_thinks_pragmatic_on_love
				years = 5
			}
		}
		scope:cynic = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:lover
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_discussion_disagree
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = scope:lover
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Real life is not like romcoms
		name = VIETmisc.0252.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_thinks_pragmatic_on_love
			years = 5
		}
		scope:cynic = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_discussion_agree
			}			
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # True love can be found through struggle
		name = VIETmisc.0252.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_thinks_love_is_struggle
			years = 5
		}
		scope:cynic = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_love_discussion_agree
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Let me eat goddammit
		name = VIETmisc.0252.c
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_dread = 5
		scope:cynic = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_like_me_talking
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_liege_awkward_talk
				years = 10
			}		
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_like_me_talking
			}	
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_liege_awkward_talk
				years = 10
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			gregarious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}

			}

				modifier = VIET_liege_didnt_like_joke
				years = 10
			}			
		}
	}

# Everything in Crusader Kings 3 can be turned into a STRUGGLE mechanic, as One Proud Bavarian says
VIETmisc.0256 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0256.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0256.desc
	theme = mental_break
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:one_proud_bavarian
		animation = schadenfreude
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:PI_dev
		animation = disapproval
	}


	trigger = {
		# OPB
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = zealous
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = ambitious
				has_trait = trusting
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = cynical
				has_trait = honest
				has_trait = content
				has_trait = stubborn
			}
		}
		# PI Dev
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = cynical
				has_trait = honest
				has_trait = content
				has_trait = stubborn
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = zealous
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = ambitious
				has_trait = trusting
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = zealous
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = ambitious
					has_trait = trusting
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = cynical
					has_trait = honest
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = stubborn
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = one_proud_bavarian
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_struggles_everywhere
				years = 10
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = cynical
					has_trait = honest
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = stubborn
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = zealous
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = ambitious
					has_trait = trusting
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = PI_dev
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_struggles_skepticism
				years = 10
			}
		}
		scope:one_proud_bavarian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:PI_dev
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = scope:PI_dev
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Anything will be turned into a struggle, Struggle is our new god
		name = VIETmisc.0256.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_struggles_everywhere
			years = 10
		}
		scope:one_proud_bavarian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_agree
			}			
		}
		scope:PI_dev = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:one_proud_bavarian
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Not everything can be turned into a struggle, silly
		name = VIETmisc.0256.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_struggles_skepticism
			years = 10
		}
		scope:one_proud_bavarian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_disagree
			}			
		}
		scope:PI_dev = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_struggle_discussion_agree
			}			
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:PI_dev
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
	}

}

# Charlemagne choir event based on the Vita Karoli Magni
# Credits to Duke Leo
VIETmisc.0257 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0257.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0257.desc
	theme = faith
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_zealous
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:chaplain
		animation = boredom
	}

	lower_center_portrait = scope:singer

	trigger = {
		religion = religion:christianity_religion
		exists = cp:councillor_court_chaplain
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			is_available_healthy_ai_adult = yes
		}
		exists = dynasty
		dynasty = {
			any_dynasty_member = {
				is_courtier_of = root
				is_adult = no
				age >= 5
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				is_ai = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			save_scope_as = chaplain
		}
		dynasty = {
			random_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					is_courtier_of = root
					is_adult = no
					age >= 5
					religion = religion:christianity_religion
					is_ai = yes
				}
				save_scope_as = singer
			}
		}		
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0257.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:chaplain = {
			increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = beaten }
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_physically_attacked_me
			}
			# random = {
			# 	chance = 50
			# 	progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			# 		CHARACTER = scope:recipient
			# 		OPINION = 0
			#		REASON = VIET_rival_reason_placeholder
			# 	}
			# }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			calm = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0257.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0257.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:singer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:chaplain
				modifier = VIET_opinion_dislikes_singing
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = medium_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0257.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0257.c
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:singer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:chaplain
				modifier = VIET_opinion_dislikes_singing
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_dislikes_singing
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0257.info
		}
	}

}




# Baklava nightmare
# Credits to Cerbzzz
VIETmisc.0258 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0258.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0258.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = corridor_night }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = fear
	}

		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		VIET_is_baklava_culture_trigger = yes
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
	}

# Teddy Roosevelt assassination reference - vassal survives assassination attempt
# Credits to Anonymous person who took the survey
VIETmisc.0259 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0259.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0259.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:teddy_roosevelt
		animation = personality_bold
	}

	trigger = {
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_healthy_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = stubborn
				has_trait = calm
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = content
			}
			NOT = {
				has_trait = craven
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_healthy_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = calm
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = content
				}
				NOT = {
					has_trait = craven
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = teddy_roosevelt
			VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_teddy_roosevelt_assassination
				years = 10
			}
			increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = assassination }
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0259.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:teddy_roosevelt = {
			VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_praised_me
			}			
		}
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0259.b
	}

}



# A traveling physician appears with a fully intact mummy
# Credits to Anonymous person who took the survey
VIETmisc.0260 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0260.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0260.desc
	theme = medicine
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = shock
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:physician
		animation = schadenfreude
	}

	# Mainly keep it to Europe and Middle East regions
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
				geographical_region = world_middle_east
				geographical_region = world_india
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = world_africa_sahara
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_middle_east
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_middle_east_persia
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_europe_south
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_europe_west_iberia
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_europe_west_francia
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_africa_north
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		every_county_in_region = {
			region = world_india_rajastan
			add_to_list = physician_counties
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = physician_counties
			save_scope_as = home_county
		}

		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_traveling_physician_template
			save_scope_as = physician
			culture = scope:home_county.culture
			faith = scope:home_county.faith
		}

	}

	
	option = { # Buy the mummy
		name = VIETmisc.0260.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_trait = cannibal }
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}

		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:physician
			gold = 50
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_mummy_medicine
			years = 15
		}

		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 75
				scope:physician = {
					death = {
						death_reason = death_vanished
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0260.info
		}

	}
	
	
	option = { # No interest
		name = VIETmisc.0260.b

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}


		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 75
				scope:physician = {
					death = {
						death_reason = death_vanished
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0260.info
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Buy the mummy as a cannibal
		name = VIETmisc.0260.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = cannibal
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}


		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:physician
			gold = 50
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_mummy_medicine
			years = 15
		}

		stress_impact = {
			cannibal = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 75
				scope:physician = {
					death = {
						death_reason = death_vanished
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0260.info
		}

	}
	
	
	option = { # Invite the Physician to stay
		name = VIETmisc.0260.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 100
				is_ai = no
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}


		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:physician
			gold = 100
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_mummy_medicine
			years = 15
		}

		set_court_physician_effect = {
			EMPLOYER = root
			PHYSICIAN = scope:physician
		}

		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0260.info
		}

	}


}

# Rumors about a bad vassal
VIETmisc.0261 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0261.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0261.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = stress
	}
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:vassal
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	trigger = {
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = vassal_candidates
		}	
		# Be more likely to pick vassals with actual flaws or likely to piss people off, but not necessarily so
		random_in_list = {
			list = vassal_candidates
			weight = {
				base = 10
				modifier = {
					has_trait = ambitious
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = sadistic
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = arbitrary
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = vengeful
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = impatient
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = paranoid
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = greedy
					add = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = lazy
					add = -1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					add = -1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = just
					add = -1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = generous
					add = -1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = gregarious
					add = -1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = temperate
					add = -1
				}
				modifier = {
					has_trait = calm
					add = -1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_nasty_rumors
				years = 10
			}
		}	
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0261.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0261.b
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = angry_opinion
				target = root
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
	}

}



# Vassal attacks a peasant
VIETmisc.0262 = {
	type = character_event

	desc = VIETmisc.0262.desc

	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = stress
	}

		animation = personality_callous
	}

		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = wrathful
				has_trait = vengeful
				has_trait = brave
				has_trait = impatient
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = calm
				has_trait = forgiving
				has_trait = craven
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = vengeful
					has_trait = brave
					has_trait = impatient
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = humble
					has_trait = calm
					has_trait = forgiving
					has_trait = craven
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_attacked_peasant_leader
				years = 6
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0262.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_vassals_attacked_peasant
			years = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0262.b
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_agreed_peasant
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_vassals_attacked_peasant
			years = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0262.c
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:vassal = {
			remove_short_term_gold = 20
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_forced_compensate_peasant
			}
		}
	}

}



# Courtier has an injury while traveling outside
VIETmisc.0263 = {
	type = character_event

	desc = VIETmisc.0263.desc
	theme = medicine
	
	#left_portrait = root
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = severelywounded
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
			increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = fall }
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0263.a
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_cares_about_me
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0263.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 20
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		stress_impact = {
			callous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_really_cares_about_me
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0263.c
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_care_about_me
			}
		}
	}

}





# Vassal is rumored to be a good leader

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0264.a
