			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0264.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = envy_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
	}

}


# Character enjoys composing vulgar music
# Credits to Anonymous person who took the 2022 survey
VIETmisc.0265 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0265.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0265.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:prude
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:musician
		animation = personality_compassionate
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = lifestyle_poet
				diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = stubborn
				has_trait = chaste
				has_trait = wrathful
				has_trait = zealous
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = stubborn
				has_trait = chaste
				has_trait = wrathful
				has_trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = lifestyle_poet
					diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = chaste
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = zealous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = musician
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_vulgar_music
				years = 9
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = chaste
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = zealous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = prude
		}
		scope:prude = {			
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:musician
				modifier = VIET_opinion_composes_vulgar_music
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = scope:musician
				modifier = VIET_opinion_dislikes_my_music
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0265.a
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:prude = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_supports_vulgar_music
			}
		}
		scope:musician = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_supports_music
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0265.b
		stress_impact = {
			honest = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:musician = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_discreet_vulgar_music
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0265.c
		stress_impact = {
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:prude = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_fellow_prude
			}
		}
		scope:musician = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_dislikes_my_music
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_composes_vulgar_music
			}
		}
	}

}

# Vassal is a robber baron
VIETmisc.0266 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0266.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0266.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = stress
	}
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:vassal
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	trigger = {
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			is_landed = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = greedy
				has_trait = arbitrary
				has_trait = ambitious
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
				has_trait = generous
				has_trait = lazy
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				is_landed = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = greedy
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = ambitious
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = just
					has_trait = generous
					has_trait = lazy
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_robber_baron
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0266.a
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lenient_robber_baron
			years = 10
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_off_the_hook
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0266.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_punished_robber_baron
			years = 10
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			remove_short_term_gold = 50
			# pay_short_term_gold = {
			# 	target = root
			# 	gold = 50
			# }
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_made_me_pay_fine
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0266.c
		add_dread = 10
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_punished_robber_baron
			years = 10
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_imprisoned_me
			}
		}
		rightfully_imprison_character_effect = {
			TARGET = scope:vassal
			IMPRISONER = root
		}
	}

}


# Vassal has a capable official who might be convinced to work for you
VIETmisc.0267 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0267.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0267.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	left_portrait = scope:vassal
	
	right_portrait = scope:official

	trigger = {
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			is_landed = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				is_landed = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
		}
		create_character = {
			employer = scope:vassal
			template = random_barrel_character
			gender_female_chance = root_faith_dominant_gender_female_chance
			faith = scope:vassal.faith
			culture = scope:vassal.culture
			save_scope_as = official
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:official = {
				random_list = {
					40 = { add_trait = shrewd }
					30 = { add_trait = intellect_good_1 }
					20 = { add_trait = intellect_good_2 }
					10 = { add_trait = intellect_good_3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0267.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = { # Failure
				desc = VIETmisc.0267.a.toast.failure
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						opinion = {
							target = scope:vassal
							value > 0
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						opinion = {
							target = scope:vassal
							value > 33
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						opinion = {
							target = scope:vassal
							value > 66
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						has_trait = content
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						has_trait = lazy
					}
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:official
					title = VIETmisc.0267.a.toast.failure
					VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
				}
			}
			50 = { # Success
				desc = VIETmisc.0267.a.toast.success
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						opinion = {
							target = scope:vassal
							value < 0
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						opinion = {
							target = scope:vassal
							value < -33
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						opinion = {
							target = scope:vassal
							value < -66
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						has_trait = ambitious
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					scope:official = {
						has_trait = greedy
					}
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:official
					title = VIETmisc.0267.a.toast.success
					add_courtier = scope:official					
					pay_short_term_gold = {
						target = scope:official
						gold = 50
					}
					scope:vassal = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_poached_official
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0267.b
		duel = {
			skill = diplomacy
			target = scope:official
			10 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -1.1
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0267.b.toast.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:official
					title = VIETmisc.0267.b.toast.failure
					VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 1.1
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0267.b.toast.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:official
					title = VIETmisc.0267.b.toast.success
					add_courtier = scope:official					
					scope:vassal = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_poached_official
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0267.c
		stress_impact = {
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}



# Vassal recently lost a lot of money and begs for help
VIETmisc.0268 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0268.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0268.desc
	theme = corruption
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_callous
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:vassal
		animation = beg
	}	

	trigger = {
		gold >= 50
		any_vassal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			gold <= 100
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				gold <= 100
			}
			save_scope_as = vassal
			remove_short_term_gold = 150
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0268.a
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_refused_to_help_my_debt_problems
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0268.b	
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:vassal
					type = indebted_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:vassal
				type = indebted_hook
			}
		}	
		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:vassal
			gold = 50
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_helped_my_debt_problems
				opinion = 15
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0268.c		
		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:vassal
			gold = 50
		}
		scope:vassal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_helped_my_debt_problems
				opinion = 50
			}
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:vassal
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}



# Courtier recently got some money and wants to give you some
VIETmisc.0269 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0269.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0269.desc
	theme = stewardship_wealth_focus
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = happiness
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = steward
	}	

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { is_close_or_extended_family_of = root }
			# Shouldn't be someone that hates you too much
			opinion = {
				target = root
				value >= -25
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { is_close_or_extended_family_of = root }
				# Shouldn't be someone that hates you too much
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= -25
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
			add_gold = 200
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0269.a
		scope:courtier = {
			pay_short_term_gold = {
				target = root
				gold = 50
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = gift_opinion
				opinion = 20
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0269.b
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:courtier = {
			pay_short_term_gold = {
				target = root
				gold = 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					can_add_hook = {
						target = root
						type = indebted_hook
					}
				}
				add_hook = {
					target = root
					type = indebted_hook
				}
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_gracious
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = gift_opinion
				opinion = 20
			}
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:courtier
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Refuse gift
		name = VIETmisc.0269.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_trait = paranoid }
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_rejected_my_gift
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Refuse gift
		name = VIETmisc.0269.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = paranoid 
		}
		trait = paranoid
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_rejected_my_gift
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}

	}

		animation = pain
	}	

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_shadowy_mysterious_woman
				years = 10
			}
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_gain
				paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
				craven = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0270.a
	}

}




# Councilor feels light-headed and requests to leave to rest, but they're needed for an important meeting
VIETmisc.0271 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0271.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0271.desc
	theme = stewardship_duty_focus
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:councilor
		animation = stress
	}	

	trigger = {
		any_councillor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_councillor = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = councilor
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_frequent_light_headedness
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0271.a
		scope:councilor = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_let_leave_meeting
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_character_modifier = VIET_frequent_light_headedness
			}
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:councilor
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0271.a.tooltip
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= high_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0271.toast.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0271.toast.success
					VIET_massive_prestige_gain_effect = yes
				}
			}
			80 = {
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0271.toast.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0271.toast.failure
					VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0271.b		
		scope:councilor = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_forced_stay_meeting
			}
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:councilor
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_rival_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0271.b.tooltip
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= high_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0271.toast.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0271.toast.success
					VIET_massive_prestige_gain_effect = yes
				}
			}
			20 = {
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0271.toast.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0271.toast.failure
					VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

}


# Councilor comes extremely tardy
VIETmisc.0272 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0272.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0272.desc
	theme = stewardship_duty_focus
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = anger
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:councilor
		animation = personality_irrational
	}	

	trigger = {
		any_councillor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = diligent
				has_trait = ambitious
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_councillor = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = diligent
					has_trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = councilor
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_tardy_to_meetings
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0272.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		scope:councilor = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_off_the_hook
			}
		}
		every_councillor = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { this = scope:councilor }
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_chastise_tardy_councilor
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0272.b
		scope:councilor = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastise_tardy
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		random = {
			chance = 30
			send_interface_toast = {
				type = event_toast_effect_good
				left_icon = ROOT
				title = VIETmisc.0272.b.tooltip
				scope:councilor = {
					remove_character_modifier = VIET_tardy_to_meetings
				}
				# if = {
				# 	limit = {
				# 		scope:councilor = {
				# 			has_trait = lazy
				# 		}
				# 	}
				# 	hidden_effect = {
				# 		remove_trait = lazy
				# 	}
				# }
				# add_trait = diligent
			}
		}
	}

}

# Boastful courtier forgets what the ten commandments are
VIETmisc.0273 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0273.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0273.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:forgetful
		animation = shame
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		OR = {
			religion = religion:christianity_religion
			religion = religion:judaism_religion
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			faith = root.faith
			OR = {
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = fickle
				has_trait = wrathful
				has_trait = ambitious
				has_trait = impatient
				has_trait = zealous
				has_trait = intellect_bad_1
				has_trait = intellect_bad_2
				has_trait = intellect_bad_3
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = cynical
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = shy
			}
			NOT = { has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				faith = root.faith
				OR = {
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = fickle
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = ambitious
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = zealous
					has_trait = intellect_bad_1
					has_trait = intellect_bad_2
					has_trait = intellect_bad_3
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = cynical
					has_trait = humble
					has_trait = shy
				}
				NOT = { has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain }
			}
			save_scope_as = forgetful
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_couldnt_remember_ten_commandments
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0273.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0273.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		#scope:forgetful = {
			# reverse_add_opinion = {
			# 	modifier = disappointed_opinion
			# 	opinion = -10
			# 	target = root
			# }
			# add_opinion = {
			# 	modifier = disappointed_opinion
			# 	opinion = -10
			# 	target = root
			# }
		#}
	}

}


# Hearing about the Roman custom of decimation
VIETmisc.0274 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0274.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0274.desc
	theme = martial_strategy_focus
	
	left_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }	
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_sahara
				geographical_region = world_middle_east
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0274.a
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0274.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0274.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = arbitrary
				has_trait = torturer
			}
		}
		trait = sadistic
		trait = arbitrary
		trait = torturer
		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes	
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = wrathful
						trait_is_sin = vengeful
						trait_is_sin = sadistic
						trait_is_sin = arbitrary
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_utilizing_decimation
			years = 15
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = massive_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = major_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}


# Learning about Tetractys
VIETmisc.0275 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0275.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0275.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:scholar
		animation = chancellor
	}

	trigger = {	
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_sahara
				geographical_region = world_middle_east
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
			}
		}
		# Weed out most cultures that probably aren't literate at the game start and wouldn't be writing stuff like letters
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	immediate = {		
		random_sub_realm_county = {
			limit = { tier = tier_county }
			save_scope_as = county
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_skilled_scholar_template
			save_scope_as = scholar
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0275.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_tetractys
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0275.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = diligent
			}
			stress_impact = {
				diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		else = {			
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_loss
				lazy = minor_stress_impact_loss
				impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
	}

	after = {		
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 75
				scope:scholar = {
					death = {
						death_reason = death_vanished
					}
				}
			}			
		}
	}

}

					diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= high_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					diplomacy >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0276.b.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0276.b.success
					VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
					scope:child = {
						add_opinion = {
							modifier = pleased_opinion
							opinion = 10
							target = root
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}




# Visiting a local school where two scholars are arguing about decimal fractions
VIETmisc.0277 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0277.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0277.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus
	override_background = { reference = garden }
		
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	trigger = {
		# Weed out most cultures that probably aren't literate and don't have scholars running around
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0277.a
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0277.b
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_learning_skill = 1
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			intellect_good_1 = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			intellect_good_2 = minor_stress_impact_gain
			intellect_good_3 = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0277.c
		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = learning
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		duel = {
			skill = learning
			value = 15
			10 = { # Failure - they're not impressed
				#show_chance = no
				custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0277.c.failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -0.7
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0277.c.failure
					VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success - interested in trade
				#show_chance = no
				custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0277.c.success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 0.7
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0277.c.success
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_impressed_mathematicians
						years = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

		}

		character = scope:grateful
		animation = personality_compassionate
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_grateful_beggar_template
			save_scope_as = grateful
		}
	}

		name = VIETmisc.0281.a

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_famous_beggar_charity_story
		}
	}

	after = {		
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:grateful = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}

}

# Maid turns the tables on manservants who try to prank her
# This idea came from a C-Drama scene
VIETmisc.0283 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0283.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0283.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = relaxing_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = throne_room_applaud_1
	}	
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:maid
		animation = laugh
	}	
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}

	immediate = {		
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_feisty_young_maid_template
			save_scope_as = maid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # haha that was funny
		name = VIETmisc.0283.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:maid = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # stop pranking her
		name = VIETmisc.0283.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:maid = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # just promote her
		name = VIETmisc.0283.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_courtier = scope:maid
	}
}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_held_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = tier_county		
				is_landless_type_title = no
			}	
			save_scope_as = county
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Tell her to get lost
		name = VIETmisc.0288.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_dismissed_karen
			years = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept her demands
		name = VIETmisc.0288.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_listened_to_karen
			years = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Tell her to get lost... diplomatically
		name = VIETmisc.0288.c
		trigger = {
			diplomacy >= very_high_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = diplomacy
		show_as_unavailable = {
			diplomacy < very_high_skill_rating
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_diplomatically_dismissed_karen
			years = 10
		}
	}

}

# Lover is not in the mood
VIETmisc.0294 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0294.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0294.desc
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = bedchamber }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:lover
		animation = dismissal
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = sadness
	}

	trigger = {
		VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
		#OR = {
		#	num_of_relation_soulmate > 0
		#	num_of_relation_lover > 0
		#}
		OR = {
			any_relation = {
				type = soulmate
				VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			any_relation = {
				type = lover
				VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				trigger = {
					any_relation = {
						type = soulmate
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
				}
				random_relation = {
					type = soulmate
					limit = {
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
					save_scope_as = lover
				}
			}
			50 = {
				trigger = {
					any_relation = {
						type = lover
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
				}
				random_relation = {
					type = lover
					limit = {
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
					save_scope_as = lover
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0294.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = lustful
			}
			stress_impact = {
				lustful = medium_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_snuggling
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_snuggling
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0294.b
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:lover = {
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_not_in_mood
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_unsatisfied_horny
			years = 3
		}
	}

}

# Crush is passing by
VIETmisc.0297 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0297.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0297.desc
	theme = romance_scheme

	
	left_portrait = scope:crush
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = shame
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
			any_vassal = {
				any_child = {
					is_available_ai_child = yes
					root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
				}
			}
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = charming
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
			add_to_list = crushes
		}
		every_vassal = {
			every_child = {
				limit = {
					is_available_ai_child = yes
					root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
				}
				add_to_list = crushes
			}
		}
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
			add_to_list = crushes
		}
				
		random_in_list = {
			list = crushes
			save_scope_as = crush
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0297.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_gain
			shy = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0297.a.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0297.a.failure
					scope:crush = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = VIET_opinion_awkward
						}
					}
				}
			}
			10 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0297.a.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0297.a.success
					scope:crush = {
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = amused_opinion
							opinion = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

# Say something insightful to your councilors as a child
VIETmisc.0300 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0300.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0300.desc
	theme = memory_formative
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:councilor
		animation = throne_room_applaud_1
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = throne_room_conversation_1
	}

	trigger = {
		any_councillor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			opinion = {
				target = root
				value >= 0
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_councillor = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = councilor
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0300.a		
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		every_councillor = {
			custom = every_councillor
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = respect_opinion
				opinion = 15
			}
		}
	}

}


# Starting to get bored of a favorite treat, and talk to an adult about it
VIETmisc.0301 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0301.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0301.desc
	theme = memory_formative
	override_background = { reference = bp1_kitchen_western }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = laugh
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_irrational
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			opinion = {
				target = root
				value >= 0
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = curious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0301.a		
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			pensive = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0301.b		
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:courtier
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_friend_reason_placeholder
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}


# Want to chase birds, but an adult says no
VIETmisc.0302 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0302.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0302.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = happiness
	}

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = lustful
				has_trait = content
				has_trait = patient
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = lustful
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = patient
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0302.a	
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_heed_me
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_boring_adult
			}
		}	
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0302.b		
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_heeded_me
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_boring_adult
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_observed_birds
			years = 5
		}	
		stress_impact = {
			rowdy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

}





# Staring at crush
VIETmisc.0303 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0303.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0303.desc
	theme = romance_scheme

	
	left_portrait = scope:crush
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = shame
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
			any_vassal = {
				any_child = {
					is_available_ai_child = yes
					root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
				}
			}
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = charming
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
			add_to_list = crushes
		}
		every_vassal = {
			every_child = {
				limit = {
					is_available_ai_child = yes
					root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
				}
				add_to_list = crushes
			}
		}
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_child = yes
				root = { has_relation_crush = prev }
			}
			add_to_list = crushes
		}
				
		random_in_list = {
			list = crushes
			save_scope_as = crush
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0303.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:crush = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = amused_opinion
				opinion = 10
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_crush_intensifying
				opinion = 20
			}
		}
	}

}



# Building sandcastles with other kids
VIETmisc.0304 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0304.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0304.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_skyrim_forest
	override_background = { reference = fp1_beached_longships }

	
	left_portrait = scope:child
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_child = yes
			age >= childhood_education_start_age
		}
		# Must have a coastal capital
		capital_county = { is_coastal_county = yes }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = charming
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_child = yes
				age >= childhood_education_start_age
			}
			save_scope_as = child
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0304.a
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_conformist_child
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			bossy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0304.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0304.b
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_not_like_the_other_children
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			charming = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:child = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = annoyed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0304.info
		}
	}

}

# Adult criticizes young girls doing medieval twerking (based on an actual medieval quote)
VIETmisc.0306 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0306.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0306.desc
	theme = party

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOR = {
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = lustful
				has_trait = content
				has_trait = humble
			}
			OR = {
				has_trait = zealous
				has_trait = arrogant
				has_trait = chaste
				has_trait = impatient
				has_trait = stubborn
				has_trait = honest
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = charming
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOR = {
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = lustful
					has_trait = content
					has_trait = humble
				}
				OR = {
					has_trait = zealous
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = chaste
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0306.a	
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes	
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				opinion = 10
				modifier = pleased_opinion
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			rowdy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0306.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0306.b	
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes	
		stress_impact = {
			rowdy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			fickle = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				opinion = 10
				modifier = pleased_opinion
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
				}
				custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0306.info
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0306.c	
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_dancing_like_hinds
			years = 5
		}	
		stress_impact = {
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				opinion = -10
				modifier = disgusted_opinion
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
				}
				custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0306.info
			}
		}
	}

}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0311.a
		add_stewardship_skill = 1
	}

}

# Two characters debate about the nature of Venus
VIETmisc.0314 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0314.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0314.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:debater_1
		animation = throne_room_conversation_3
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:debater_2
		animation = laugh
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				count >= 2
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				count >= 2
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			add_to_list = debate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			add_to_list = debate_characters
		}
		ordered_in_list = {
			list = debate_characters
			max = 2
			check_range_bounds = no
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:debater_1 }
				}
				save_scope_as = debater_1
			}
			else = {
				save_scope_as = debater_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:debater_1 = {
					can_set_relation_friend_trigger = { CHARACTER = scope:debater_2 }
				}
			}
			scope:debater_1 = {
				set_relation_friend = { reason = VIET_natural_philosophy_interest target = scope:debater_2 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0314.a
		scope:debater_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_agrees_intellectual
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:debater_2
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_natural_philosophy_interest
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_description_no_bullet = {
				text = VIETmisc.0314.info
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0314.b
		scope:debater_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_agrees_intellectual
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:debater_1
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_natural_philosophy_interest
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_description_no_bullet = {
				text = VIETmisc.0314.info
			}
		}
	}

}

# Boring character likes to talk about the moon
VIETmisc.0316 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0316.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0316.desc
	theme = diplomacy 

	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:boring
		animation = happiness
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
				diplomacy <= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOT = { has_trait = gregarious }
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
				diplomacy <= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOT = { has_trait = gregarious }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
				diplomacy <= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOT = { has_trait = gregarious }
			}
			add_to_list = boring_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
				diplomacy <= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOT = { has_trait = gregarious }
			}
			add_to_list = boring_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = boring_characters
			save_scope_as = boring
		}
		scope:boring = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_boring_astronomy_interest
				years = 15
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0316.a
		scope:boring = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = hurt_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}			
		}
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			custom = VIET_every_courtier_guest_unintellectual
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = grateful_opinion
				opinion = 5
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:boring
				modifier = bored_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0316.b
		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating
		}
		skill = learning		
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_impressed_others_with_knowledge
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0316.c
		trigger = {
			learning < decent_skill_rating
		}	
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes		
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			custom = VIET_every_courtier_guest_unintellectual
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:boring
				modifier = bored_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}	
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0316.c.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0316.c.failure
					stress_impact = {
						base = minor_stress_impact_gain
					}	
				}
			}
			10 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0316.c.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0316.c.success
					add_learning_skill = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

# Two characters debate about the reliability of astrology
VIETmisc.0318 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0318.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0318.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:debater_1
		animation = throne_room_conversation_3
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:debater_2
		animation = laugh
	}

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				count >= 2
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
			}
			any_vassal = {
				count >= 2
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
			}
			add_to_list = debate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
			}
			add_to_list = debate_characters
		}
		ordered_in_list = {
			list = debate_characters
			max = 2
			check_range_bounds = no
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:debater_1 }
				}
				save_scope_as = debater_1
			}
			else = {
				save_scope_as = debater_2
			}
		}
		scope:debater_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:debater_2
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = scope:debater_2
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0318.a
		scope:debater_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_agrees_intellectual
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:debater_1
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_natural_philosophy_interest
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_description_no_bullet = {
				text = VIETmisc.0318.info
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0318.b
		scope:debater_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_agrees_intellectual
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:debater_2
			OPINION = 0
			REASON = VIET_natural_philosophy_interest
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_description_no_bullet = {
				text = VIETmisc.0318.info
			}
		}
	}

}


# Dog Days caused by Sirius
# Triggered by ping event VIETintro.1000 to get the timing roughly right
VIETmisc.0319 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0319.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0319.desc
	theme = medicine
	override_background = { reference = garden }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:physician
		animation = reading
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = pain
	}

	trigger = {
		court_physician_available_trigger = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		save_court_physician_as_effect = { SCOPE_NAME = physician }
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0319.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 50
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_description_no_bullet = {
				text = VIETmisc.0319.info
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0319.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_sirius_dog_days
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_description_no_bullet = {
				text = VIETmisc.0319.info
			}
		}
	}

}

# Repenting after saying some swears
VIETmisc.0320 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0320.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0320.desc
	theme = unfriendly

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = shame
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:chaplain
		animation = disapproval
	}


	trigger = {
		religion = religion:christianity_religion
		exists = cp:councillor_court_chaplain
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			is_available_healthy_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
	}


	immediate = {
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			save_scope_as = chaplain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0320.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_repent_bread_water
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gluttonous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		scope:chaplain = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 10
				target = root
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0320.b
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		scope:chaplain = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -10
				target = root
			}
		}
	}


	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0320.info
		}
	}


}

# Courtier overdoses on marking nuts
VIETmisc.0325 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0325.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0325.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:overdosed
		animation = sick
	}


	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= decent_skill_rating

			}
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
		}
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_middle_east
				geographical_region = world_india
				geographical_region = world_africa_north
				geographical_region = world_africa_east
				geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
			add_to_list = candidates
		}
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= decent_skill_rating
			}
			add_to_list = candidates
		}
				
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidates
			save_scope_as = overdosed
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_overdosed_on_marking_nuts
						years = 4
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_overdosed_on_marking_nuts
						years = 8
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_overdosed_on_marking_nuts
						years = 12
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_overdosed_on_marking_nuts
						years = 16
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_overdosed_on_marking_nuts
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0325.a
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:overdosed = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_no_sympathy
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0325.b
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:overdosed = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_sympathy
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}

	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0325.info
		}
	}


}

VIETmisc.0329 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0329.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0329.desc

	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:gardener
		animation = happiness
	}


	trigger = {
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = ghw_region_subsahelian_africa
				geographical_region = custom_lanka
			}
		}
		
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = lifestyle_gardener
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = lifestyle_gardener
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = lifestyle_gardener
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			add_to_list = gardener_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = lifestyle_gardener
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			add_to_list = gardener_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = gardener_characters
			save_scope_as = gardener
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0329.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
		scope:gardener = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_impressed_others_with_knowledge
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0329.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_learning_about_old_world_cactus
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:gardener = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_impressed_others_with_knowledge
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0329.info
		}

	}
	


}

		animation = thinking
	}

		character = scope:kind
		animation = happiness
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		# capital_province = {
		# 	OR = {
		# 		terrain = desert
		# 		terrain = desert_mountains
		# 	}
		# }
		OR = {
			religion = religion:islam_religion

			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = generous
					has_trait = just
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = sadistic }
				NOT = { has_trait = callous }
				NOT = { has_trait = arbitrary }
				OR = {
					religion = religion:islam_religion
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian }
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = generous
					has_trait = just
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = sadistic }
				NOT = { has_trait = callous }
				NOT = { has_trait = arbitrary }
				OR = {
					religion = religion:islam_religion
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = generous
					has_trait = just
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = sadistic }
				NOT = { has_trait = callous }
				NOT = { has_trait = arbitrary }
				OR = {
					religion = religion:islam_religion
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian }
				}
			}
			add_to_list = kind_candidates
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = generous
					has_trait = just
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = sadistic }
				NOT = { has_trait = callous }
				NOT = { has_trait = arbitrary }
				OR = {
					religion = religion:islam_religion
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian }
				}
			}
			add_to_list = kind_candidates
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = kind_candidates
			weight = {
				base = 10
				modifier = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					add = 10
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_benevolent_jinn_encounter
				years = 25
			}
			save_scope_as = kind
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Okay
		name = VIETmisc.0330.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_heard_fantasy_stories
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Okay
		name = VIETmisc.0330.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_skeptical_about_fantasy_stories
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	

	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0330.info
		}
	}
}




##################################################################
