# Anglo-Saxon double entendre riddle about keys
VIETmisc.0331 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0331.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0331.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = courtyard }

	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:joker
		animation = laugh
	}


	trigger = {		
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				# Shouldn't be a dumbass
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
				diplomacy >= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				# Shouldn't be a dumbass
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
				diplomacy >= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				# Shouldn't be a dumbass
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
				diplomacy >= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				# Shouldn't be a dumbass
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
				diplomacy >= mediocre_skill_rating
				NOR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = joker
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0331.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 365
		}
		scope:joker = {
			VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_like_my_joke
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_good_joke
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0331.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_unamused_ruler
			days = 365
		}
		scope:joker = {
			VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_like_my_joke
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_bad_joke
			}				
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_liege_didnt_like_joke
				years = 10
			}	
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0331.info
		}

	}
	


}


# Joke about the self-castrating husband, from Facetiae, a 15th century Italian joke book
VIETmisc.0332 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0332.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0332.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = courtyard }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier_1
		animation = personality_irrational
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier_2
		animation = eyeroll
	}


	trigger = {	
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			count >= 2
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = courtier_candidates
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = courtier_candidates
			save_scope_as = courtier_1
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = courtier_candidates
			limit = {
				exists = scope:courtier_1
				NOT = { this = scope:courtier_1 }
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier_2
		}
		scope:courtier_1 = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_embarrassing_misunderstanding
				years = 10
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:courtier_2
				modifier = humiliated_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0332.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = humiliated_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0332.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 365
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0332.info
		}

	}
	


}


# Cicero's anecdote about the crappy orator
VIETmisc.0333 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0333.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0333.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:councillor_1
		animation = chancellor
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:councillor_2
		animation = boredom
	}


	trigger = {	
		any_councillor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			count >= 2
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_councillor = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = councillor_candidates
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = councillor_candidates
			save_scope_as = councillor_1
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = councillor_candidates
			limit = {
				exists = scope:councillor_1
				NOT = { this = scope:councillor_1 }
			}
			save_scope_as = councillor_2
		}
		scope:councillor_1 = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_boring_speaker
				years = 10
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:councillor_2
				modifier = angry_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
		scope:councillor_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:councillor_1
				modifier = VIET_opinion_terrible_speech
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0333.a
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			patient = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:councillor_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = humiliated_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_terrible_speech
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0333.b
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:councillor_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_supported_me
			}
		}
		scope:councillor_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastised_me_in_public
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0333.info
		}

	}
	


}



# Philogelos quip about sea travel
VIETmisc.0334 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0334.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0334.desc
	theme = travel
	override_background = { reference = docks }

	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = scope:courtier_1


	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = eccentric
					has_trait = lazy
				}
				NOT = {
					has_trait = brave
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = eccentric
					has_trait = lazy
				}
				NOT = {
					has_trait = brave
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = eccentric
					has_trait = lazy
				}
				NOT = {
					has_trait = brave
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = stubborn
					has_trait = eccentric
					has_trait = lazy
				}
				NOT = {
					has_trait = brave
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier_1
		}
		scope:courtier_1 = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_travel_afraid
				years = 20
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0334.a
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			years = 3
		}
		scope:courtier_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_appreciated_wit
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_touche
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0334.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = annoyed_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = dismissive_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0334.info
		}

	}
	


}

		}
		modifier = {

	}

	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0337.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_mouse_herbal_incense
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0337.b
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0337.info
		}
	}	


}





# Child is told Aesop fable involving a cunning cat and mice
VIETmisc.0338 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0338.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0338.desc
	theme = memory_formative

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:guardian
		animation = happy_teacher
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}

	trigger = {
		any_relation = {
			type = guardian
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_relation = {
			type = guardian
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = guardian
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0338.a
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:guardian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_paid_attention
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			bossy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0338.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:guardian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_paid_attention
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			rowdy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0338.c
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:guardian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_paid_attention
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			charming = minor_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0338.d
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:guardian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_pay_attention
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
			rowdy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0338.info
		}
	}	

}

		}

		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}

			add = -0.2

		}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2

		}

# Lambast - councilor criticizes another councilor for dozing off at a meeting # _captainnemo
VIETmisc.0342 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0342.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0342.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:councilor_1
		animation = shame
	}
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:councilor_2
		animation = disapproval
	}


	trigger = {	
		any_councillor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			count >= 2
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = forgiving
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = vengeful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_councillor = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = councilor_candidates
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = councilor_candidates
			save_scope_as = councilor_1
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = councilor_candidates
			limit = {
				exists = scope:councilor_1
				NOT = { this = scope:councilor_1 }
			}
			save_scope_as = councilor_2
		}
		scope:councilor_1 = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_embarrassing_situation
				years = 10
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:councilor_2
				modifier = VIET_opinion_lambasted_me
			}
		}
		scope:councilor_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = scope:councilor_1
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shirks_duties
			}
			progress_towards_rival_effect = {
				CHARACTER = scope:councilor_1
				OPINION = 0
				REASON = VIET_rival_reason_placeholder
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0342.a
		scope:councilor_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_stood_up
			}
		}
		scope:councilor_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0342.b
		scope:councilor_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_lambasted_me
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shirks_duties
			}
		}
		scope:councilor_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 10
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0342.c
		scope:councilor_1 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = annoyed_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
		scope:councilor_2 = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = annoyed_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}
	


}


# Snuggery - courtier suggests you set aside a room as a snuggery for relaxing # Cerbzzz
VIETmisc.0343 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0343.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0343.desc
	theme = memory_positive
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = throne_room_conversation_2
	}
	right_portrait = root


	trigger = {	
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_snuggery_modifier }	
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}


	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0343.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 50
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_snuggery_modifier
			years = 20
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_listened_to_my_advice
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_good_advice
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0343.b
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}


}

# Courtier gains an interest in marine biology
VIETmisc.0344 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0344.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0344.desc
	theme = memory_learning
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = thinking
	}

	trigger = {
		any_held_county = {
			is_landless_type_title = no
			is_coastal_county = yes	
		}
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					learning >= decent_skill_rating
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_maritime_animal_knowledge
				years = 12
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0344.a
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0344.b
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0344.info
		}
	}
	


}

			modifier = VIET_doesnt_fear_risks
			years = 6
		}
		stress_impact = {
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0346.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_minimizes_risks
			years = 6
		}
		stress_impact = {
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			brave = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	after = {			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0346.info
		}
	}
	


}

# Scholar gives a lecture on triangles
VIETmisc.0347 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0347.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0347.desc
	theme = learning_scholarship_focus
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}

	trigger = {
		# Want someone who's probably literate
		probably_unintelligent_trigger = no
		# Weed out most cultures that probably aren't literate at the game start and wouldn't be doing formal mathematics
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0347.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_learning_math
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0347.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_indoors_nap
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	after = {		
		every_courtier = {
			custom = VIET_intellectual_courtiers
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				probably_unintelligent_trigger = no
				learning >= low_skill_rating
				OR = {
					has_trait = diligent
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = theologian
					has_trait = education_learning_1
					has_trait = education_learning_2
					has_trait = education_learning_3
					has_trait = education_learning_4
					learning >= medium_skill_rating
					stewardship >= medium_skill_rating
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = lazy }
				NOT = { has_trait = arbitrary }
				NOT = { has_trait = impatient }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_learning_math
				years = 3
			}	
		}
		every_courtier = {
			custom = VIET_unintellectual_courtiers
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				probably_unintelligent_trigger = no
				learning <= medium_skill_rating
				OR = {
					has_trait = lazy
					has_trait = arbitrary
					has_trait = impatient
					learning <= low_skill_rating
					probably_unintelligent_trigger = yes
				}
				NOT = { has_trait = scholar }
				NOT = { has_trait = theologian }
				NOT = { has_trait = education_learning_1 }
				NOT = { has_trait = education_learning_2 }
				NOT = { has_trait = education_learning_3 }
				NOT = { has_trait = education_learning_4 }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_indoors_nap
				years = 3
			}		
		}
	}
	


}

# Child is taught about the Three Jewels of Buddhism
VIETmisc.0349 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0349.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0349.desc
	theme = memory_formative

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:guardian
		animation = happy_teacher
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}

	trigger = {
		religion = religion:buddhism_religion
		any_relation = {
			type = guardian
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = pensive
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_relation = {
			type = guardian
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes				
				religion = religion:buddhism_religion
			}
			save_scope_as = guardian
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0349.a
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:guardian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_paid_attention
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			bossy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0349.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:guardian = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_pay_attention
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
			rowdy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}

}

# Running low on firewood at a camp, but there are spirits nearby
VIETmisc.0351 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0351.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0351.desc
	theme = laamp
	override_background = { reference = bp1_bonfire }
	
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = marshal_axe
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:superstitious
		animation = stayback
	}

	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_travelling = no
				domicile ?= {
					domicile_location = {
						NOR = {
							terrain = drylands
							terrain = desert
							terrain = desert_mountains
							terrain = oasis
						}
					}
				}
				any_courtier = {
					is_available_ai_adult = yes
					NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
					OR = {
						has_trait = zealous
						has_trait = paranoid
						has_trait = eccentric
						has_trait = gregarious
						has_trait = craven
						has_trait = fickle
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_travelling = yes
				location = {
					NOR = {
						terrain = drylands
						terrain = desert
						terrain = desert_mountains
						terrain = oasis
					}					
				}
				current_travel_plan ?= {
					any_entourage_character = {	
						is_ai = yes
						is_available_travelling = yes
						NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
						OR = {
							has_trait = zealous
							has_trait = paranoid
							has_trait = eccentric
							has_trait = gregarious
							has_trait = craven
							has_trait = fickle
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			domicile ?= {
				domicile_location = {
					OR = {
						terrain = forest
						terrain = jungle
						terrain = mountains
						terrain = hills
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_travelling = yes
				exists = current_travel_plan
			}
			current_travel_plan ?= {
				random_entourage_character = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
						is_available_travelling = yes
						NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
						OR = {
							has_trait = zealous
							has_trait = paranoid
							has_trait = eccentric
							has_trait = gregarious
							has_trait = craven
							has_trait = fickle
						}
					}
					save_scope_as = superstitious
				}	
			}	
			location.county = { save_scope_as = county }
			scope:county.culture = {
				save_scope_as = culture
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_available_ai_adult = yes
					NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
					OR = {
						has_trait = zealous
						has_trait = paranoid
						has_trait = eccentric
						has_trait = gregarious
						has_trait = craven
						has_trait = fickle
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = superstitious
			}
			root.domicile.domicile_location.county = {
				save_scope_as = county
			}
			scope:county.culture = {
				save_scope_as = culture
			}
		}

	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0351.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 10
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 10
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0351.b
		random_list = {
			100 = {
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0351.b.nothing
				send_interface_toast = {
					title = VIETmisc.0351.b.nothing
					left_icon = root
					type = event_toast_effect_good
				}
			}
			100 = {
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0351.b.bad
				send_interface_toast = {
					title = VIETmisc.0351.b.bad
					left_icon = root
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_forest_spirit_curse
						years = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	


}

# Merchant returns after encountering people who never knew about henna and hair dye, and tells exaggerated tale
VIETmisc.0353 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0353.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0353.desc
	theme = diplomacy_foreign_affairs_focus
	

	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_content
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:merchant
		animation = storyteller
	}

	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		VIET_is_henna_culture_trigger = yes
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				template = VIET_traveling_merchant_template_male
				culture = root.culture
				faith = root.faith
				save_scope_as = merchant		
			}
			scope:merchant = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_well_traveled_merchant
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Exaggerated tale
		name = VIETmisc.0353.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:merchant = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Wow cool!
		name = VIETmisc.0353.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:merchant = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Invite him to stay
		name = VIETmisc.0353.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 40
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 40
		add_courtier = scope:merchant
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0353.info
		}
	}

}

			modifier = VIET_quality_henna
			years = 8
		}
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			chaste = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0354.info
		}
	}

}

		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}

		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		# Should not happen to cultures where redheads could feasibly appear in large enough numbers
		culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = no
		#culture_has_mena_heritage_pillar_trigger = no
		culture_has_north_african_heritage_pillar_trigger = no
		# Should not happen in locations with those kinds of cultures
		capital_province = {
			NOR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = world_steppe_west
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor

				geographical_region = world_middle_east_jerusalem

		}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}

			add = -0.2

		}

		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2

# Conversation about Judas Iscariot's red hair
VIETmisc.0356 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0356.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0356.desc
	theme = diplomacy_foreign_affairs_focus
	

	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = throne_room_conversation_4
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:antisemite
		animation = throne_room_conversation_2
	}


	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
		religion = religion:christianity_religion
		NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = antisemite
		}
		scope:antisemite = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_distrusts_jews
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We wouldn't know
		name = VIETmisc.0356.a
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Yeah, he was probably a redhead
		name = VIETmisc.0356.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_distrusts_jews
			years = 10
		}
		scope:antisemite = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 10
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Maybe Jesus was a redhead
		name = VIETmisc.0356.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_showed_sympathy_to_jews
			years = 10
		}
		scope:antisemite = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -10
			}
		}
	}


}




# Favorite hair color?
VIETmisc.0357 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0357.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0357.desc
	theme = diplomacy_foreign_affairs_focus
	
	cooldown = { years = 25 }

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}

	lower_left_portrait = {
		character = scope:blonde
	}

	lower_center_portrait = {
		character = scope:redhead
	}

	lower_right_portrait = {
		character = scope:brunette
	}


	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		exists = capital_province # To prevent error messages below
		OR = {
			VIET_is_redhead_or_blonde_area_or_culture = yes
			VIET_is_redhead_or_blonde_area_capital = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_trait = celibate }
		NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				count >= 3 # Need at least three courtiers
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				VIET_is_redhead_or_blonde_area_or_culture = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = celibate }
				NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				VIET_is_redhead_or_blonde_area_or_culture = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = celibate }
				NOT = { has_sexuality = asexual }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				religion = religion:christianity_religion
				NOT = {	culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite } }
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = blonde
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			limit = {
				exists = scope:blonde
				NOT = { this = scope:blonde }
			}
			save_scope_as = redhead
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			limit = {
				exists = scope:blonde
				exists = scope:redhead
				NOT = { this = scope:blonde }
				NOT = { this = scope:redhead }
			}
			save_scope_as = brunette
		}
	}
	
	option = { # blonde
		name = VIETmisc.0357.a
		scope:blonde = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 5
			}
		}
		scope:redhead = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
		scope:brunette = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # redhead
		name = VIETmisc.0357.b
		scope:redhead = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 5
			}
		}
		scope:blonde = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
		scope:brunette = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # brunette
		name = VIETmisc.0357.c
		scope:brunette = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				opinion = 5
			}
		}
		scope:blonde = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
		scope:redhead = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -5
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # None
		name = VIETmisc.0357.d
	}


}

# Follow up to VIETmisc.0030: Tripped and fell while saying farewell to an envoy
# Rumors and stories spreading about your tripping
VIETmisc.0358 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0358.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0358.desc
	theme = diplomacy_foreign_affairs_focus
	

	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = stress
	}


	trigger = {	
		is_landed_or_landless_administrative = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_embarrassing_incident_rumors
			years = 10
		}
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_stress 
	}

	option = { # Grr
		name = VIETmisc.0358.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Suppress it
		name = VIETmisc.0358.b
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		duel = {
			skills = { diplomacy intrigue }
			value = average_skill_rating
			50 = { # It doesn't work
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0358.b.toast.fail
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -2.5
					min = -49
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					title = VIETmisc.0358.b.toast.fail	
					add_legitimacy = miniscule_legitimacy_loss
					remove_character_modifier = VIET_embarrassing_incident_rumors
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_embarrassing_incident_rumors_suppression_fail
						years = 10
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { # It works
				show_chance = no
				desc = VIETmisc.0358.b.toast.success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 2.5
					min = -49
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					title = VIETmisc.0358.b.toast.success	
					remove_character_modifier = VIET_embarrassing_incident_rumors
				}
			}
		}
	}


}

# Discuss a legend about how the rose got its thorns with a courtier
VIETmisc.0361 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0361.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0361.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	

	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_content
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = storyteller
	}

	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_abrahamic }
			religion = religion:zoroastrianism_religion
			NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events }
		}
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating	
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating	
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating	
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				learning >= mediocre_skill_rating	
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Truth
		name = VIETmisc.0361.a
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Exaggerated
		name = VIETmisc.0361.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I know something about flowers....
		name = VIETmisc.0361.c
		trigger = {
			learning >= medium_skill_rating			
		}	
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_impressed_others_with_knowledge
			days = 365
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}

	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0361.info
		}
	}

}



# Physician suggests a tonic based on rosemary flowers
VIETmisc.0362 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0362.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0362.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_garden_generic
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:physician
		animation = physician
	}
	
	trigger = {
		court_physician_available_trigger = yes
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_court_physician_as_effect = { SCOPE_NAME = physician }
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0362.a

			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no

		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_rosemary_flower_tonic
			years = 10
		}		
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0362.b		
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	

	
	after = {		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}

		}
	}

# Eating candied flowers
VIETmisc.0363 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0363.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0363.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_kitchen_generic

	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Weed out most cultures that are less settled at the game start and wouldn't have confectioners like this
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }	
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0363.a				
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}	

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0363.b	
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 30
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 30	
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_candied_flowers
			years = 7
		}					
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	



}



# Lover offers you flowers one day
VIETmisc.0364 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0364.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0364.desc
	theme = love
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_tuscan_country }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:lover
		animation = flirtation
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			any_relation = {
				type = lover
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				count >= 1
			}			
			any_relation = {
				type = soulmate
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				count >= 1
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_relation = {
			type = lover
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_relation = {
			type = soulmate
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = lover
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0364.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_wildflowers_gift
			days = 800
		}
		add_opinion = {
			target = scope:lover
			modifier = love_opinion
			opinion = 10
		}
	}	

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0364.b	
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 15
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_wildflowers_gift
			days = 800
		}
		add_opinion = {
			target = scope:lover
			modifier = love_opinion
			opinion = 10
		}	
		scope:lover = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_wildflowers_gift
				days = 800
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = love_opinion
				opinion = 10
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	



}



# You and a lover enjoy playing with some flowers one day
VIETmisc.0365 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0365.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0365.desc
	theme = love
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_skyrim_forest }

	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = admiration
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:lover
		animation = happiness
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			any_relation = {
				type = lover
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				count >= 1
			}			
			any_relation = {
				type = soulmate
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				count >= 1
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_relation = {
			type = lover
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_relation = {
			type = soulmate
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = lover
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = love_opinion
				opinion = 10
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = love_opinion
				opinion = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0365.a
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}	

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0365.b	
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}	



}




##################################################################
# SNOW 0366-0368

# Courtier gets stuck outside in a snowstorm and returns
VIETmisc.0366 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0366.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0366.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	override_background = { reference = VIET_background_snowy_winter_wonderland }
	

	# left_portrait = {
	# 	character = root
	# 	animation = shock
	# }

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = shiver
	}

	widget = {
		gui = "event_window_widget_vfx_snow"
		container = "foreground_shader_vfx_container"
	}

	trigger = {	
		location_has_winter_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = ill } 
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = ill } 
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = ill } 
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = ill } 
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # glad you're okay
		name = VIETmisc.0366.a
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_sympathy
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { # whatever
		name = VIETmisc.0366.b
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_no_sympathy
			}			
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		
		scope:courtier = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_gain
				lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			}
			show_as_tooltip = { add_trait = ill }
			hidden_effect = {
				#Adds the trait, sends event "health.2201" to those who care if health is brought too low
				contract_disease_effect = {
					DISEASE = ill
					TREATMENT_EVENT = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

		}

					has_trait = depressed
					has_trait = lunatic
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = intellect_bad_1
					has_trait = intellect_bad_2
					has_trait = intellect_bad_3
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = eccentric
					has_trait = possessed
					has_trait = depressed
					has_trait = lunatic
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = intellect_bad_1
					has_trait = intellect_bad_2
					has_trait = intellect_bad_3
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters

		random_in_list = {

		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_obsessed_with_eating_snow

		# 		}
		# 		NOT = {
		# 			has_trait = forgiving
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	add_to_list = candidate_characters
		# }
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = accident }
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_coconut_head_injury
				years = 4
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # locals should compensate
		name = VIETmisc.0371.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_coconut_injury_supported_courtier
			years = 10
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_sympathy
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { # locals do not need to compensate
		name = VIETmisc.0371.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_coconut_injury_supported_locals
			years = 10
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_no_sympathy
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { # you will compensate the courtier yourself
		name = VIETmisc.0371.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:courtier
			gold = 50
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_coconut_injury_paid_compensation
			years = 10
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_showed_sympathy
			}		
		}
	}

	
}

# Hagaer - A bookworm in the Imperial City
VIETmisc.0372 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0372.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0372.desc
	theme = feast_activity

	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:hagaer
		animation = reading
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 18 30 }
				gender_female_chance = root_faith_dominant_gender_adjusted_female_chance
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = hagaer
				random_traits = no
				trait = education_learning_3
				trait = shy
				trait = trusting
				trait = eccentric				
			}
			scope:hagaer = {
				VIET_ek_character_setup_effect = yes
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_hagaer_modifier
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0372.a		
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:hagaer = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}	

	option = { # You look handy
		name = VIETmisc.0372.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 50
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		pay_short_term_gold = {
			target = scope:hagaer
			gold = 50
		}
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			vengeful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}		
		add_courtier = scope:hagaer
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:hagaer
					type = loyalty_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:hagaer
				type = loyalty_hook
			}
		}
	}	

	option = { # Pay books for him
		name = VIETmisc.0372.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 25
				is_ai = no
			}
			has_trait = generous
		}
		trait = generous

		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_supports_bookworms
			years = 8
		}
		
		stress_impact = {
			scholar = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			scope:hagaer = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}	
}

# Reading one of the Thirty-Six Strategems about sacrificing the plum tree to preserve the peach tree
VIETmisc.0375 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0375.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0375.desc
	theme = martial_strategy_focus
	override_background = {
		reference = study
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = reading
	}

	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
		# Want someone who's probably literate and not a dumbass
		NOT = { has_trait = blind }
		probably_unintelligent_trigger = no
		OR = {
			probably_intelligent_trigger = yes
			diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating
			martial >= decent_skill_rating
			learning >= decent_skill_rating
		}
		# Weed out most cultures that probably aren't literate at the game start and wouldn't be writing stuff like letters
		NOT = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}	

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0375.a		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_36_stratagems_peach_military
			years = 10
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0375.b		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_36_stratagems_peach_intrigue
			years = 10
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0375.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		trait = gluttonous
		stress_impact = {
			gluttonous = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_ate_good_food
			days = 456
		}
	}	

}

	}

		character = scope:physician
		animation = debating
	}
	
	trigger = {
		court_physician_available_trigger = yes
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_court_physician_as_effect = { SCOPE_NAME = physician }
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0376.a

				gold >= 20
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_healthy_peaches
			years = 8
		}
		scope:physician = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_listened_to_my_advice
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_good_advice
			}
		}

	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0376.b
		scope:physician = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = disappointed_opinion
				opinion = -10
				target = root
			}
		}

	}	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0376.info
		}
	}

}


# Hanging peach wood talismans around the house

	}

				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
				opinion = {
					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2

		}

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = vengeful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = forgiving
		}
	}

		every_courtier_or_guest = {

				is_available_ai_adult = yes

					target = root
					value >= 0
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes

					target = root
					value >= 0
				}

		}
	}

				gold >= 25

			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 25
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_peach_wood_talismans
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_listened_to_my_advice
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_good_advice
			}
		}

	option = { # Ok

			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain

		}

# Lover tells lame jokes about peaches
VIETmisc.0378 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0378.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0378.desc
	theme = friendly
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = frontend_right_idle
	}

	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:lover
		animation = laugh
	}
	
	trigger = {
		VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
		#OR = {
		#	num_of_relation_soulmate > 0
		#	num_of_relation_lover > 0
		#}
		OR = {
			any_relation = {
				type = soulmate
				VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			any_relation = {
				type = lover
				VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				trigger = {
					any_relation = {
						type = soulmate
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
				}
				random_relation = {
					type = soulmate
					limit = {
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
					save_scope_as = lover
				}
			}
			50 = {
				trigger = {
					any_relation = {
						type = lover
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
				}
				random_relation = {
					type = lover
					limit = {
						VIET_sexual_character_trigger = yes
						is_available_ai_adult = yes
					}
					save_scope_as = lover
				}
			}
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_likes_lame_jokes
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0378.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_doesnt_like_lame_jokes
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_dislikes_my_lame_jokes
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_annoying_lame_jokes
			}
		}

	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0378.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_likes_lame_jokes
			years = 5
		}
		stress_impact = {
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:lover = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_likes_my_lame_jokes
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_amused_by_lame_jokes
			}
		}

	}	


}

}


# Have a dream where supposedly a courtier stole the peaches of immortality in a past life
VIETmisc.0380 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0380.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0380.desc
	theme = memory_intrigue
	override_background = { reference = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = scope:courtier
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		is_landed = yes
		OR = {
			culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
			religion = religion:taoism_religion
		}
		OR = {
			any_courtier_or_guest = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
					religion = religion:taoism_religion
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
					religion = religion:taoism_religion
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = eccentric
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
					religion = religion:taoism_religion
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		every_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					culture_has_east_asian_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes
					religion = religion:taoism_religion
				}
			}
			add_to_list = candidate_characters
		}
		random_in_list = {
			list = candidate_characters
			save_scope_as = courtier
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_dongfang_shuo
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0380.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_skeptical_ruler
			years = 5
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0380.b
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastised_me_in_public
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0380.c
		scope:courtier = {
			VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_nascent_spiritual_powers
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_thinks_i_have_spiritual_powers
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0380.info
		}
	}

}
