# Chancellor proposes keeping a closer eye on envoys' servants
VIETmisc.0381 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0381.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0381.desc
	theme = diplomacy_foreign_affairs_focus
	override_background = { reference = council_chamber }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:chancellor
		animation = debating
	}

	trigger = {	
		is_landed = yes
		exists = cp:councillor_chancellor
		cp:councillor_chancellor = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		cp:councillor_chancellor = {
			save_scope_as = chancellor
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # Let's be careful of them
		name = VIETmisc.0381.a	
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_suspicious_of_envoys_attendants
			years = 8
		}
		stress_impact = {
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
			honest = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:chancellor = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_envoys_advice_good
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # We can trust them
		name = VIETmisc.0381.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_generous_towards_envoys_attendants
			years = 8
		}
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			deceitful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:chancellor = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_envoys_advice_bad
			}
		}
	}	

}


# Marshal doesn't care about diviners (also, Saladin quote from Kingdom of Heaven)
VIETmisc.0382 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0382.t
	window = big_event_window
	desc = VIETmisc.0382.desc
	theme = memory_martial
	override_background = { reference = army_camp }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:marshal
		animation = personality_callous
	}

	trigger = {	
		exists = cp:councillor_marshal
		cp:councillor_marshal = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			martial >= medium_skill_rating
			faith = root.faith
			NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
			NOT = { has_trait = trusting }
			NOT = { has_trait = craven }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		cp:councillor_marshal = {
			save_scope_as = marshal
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_skeptical_of_military_diviners
				years = 25
			}
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # I trust you over diviners
		name = VIETmisc.0382.a
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes	
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:marshal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_agrees_intellectual
			}
		}	
	}	
	
	option = { # Be nicer to the diviners
		name = VIETmisc.0382.b
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes	
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:marshal = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disagrees_intellectual
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Use diviners to boost morale
		name = VIETmisc.0382.c
		duel = {
			skills = { diplomacy martial }
			target = scope:marshal
			10 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -0.8
					min = -49
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0382.c.toast.failure
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:marshal
					title = VIETmisc.0382.c.toast.failure
					scope:marshal = {	
						add_opinion = {
							target = root
							modifier = annoyed_opinion
							opinion = -15
						}
					}	
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 0.8
					min = -49
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0382.c.toast.success
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:marshal
					title = VIETmisc.0382.c.toast.success
					scope:marshal = {
						add_opinion = { 
							target = root
							opinion = 15
							modifier = fp3_convincing_argument_opinion
						}				
						add_character_modifier = {
							modifier = VIET_diviners_boost_military_morale
							years = 15
						}						
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0382.info
		}
	}

}



# Spymaster says there's an opportunity to hire a commoner servant family to spy on other nobles
VIETmisc.0383 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0383.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0383.desc
	theme = intrigue_skulduggery_focus
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:spymaster
		animation = scheme
	}

	trigger = {	
		exists = cp:councillor_spymaster
		cp:councillor_spymaster = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		cp:councillor_spymaster = {
			save_scope_as = spymaster
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # Hire them
		name = VIETmisc.0383.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 60
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 60
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_espionage_network_of_commoners
			years = 15
		}	
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			honest = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:spymaster = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_espionage_advice_good
			}
		}	
	}	
	
	option = { # Don't hire them
		name = VIETmisc.0383.b
		stress_impact = {
			deceitful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:spymaster = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_espionage_advice_bad
			}
		}	
	}	

}



# Court Chaplain has doubts about their theological knowledge
VIETmisc.0384 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0384.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0384.desc
	theme = learning_theology_focus
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		triggered_animation = {
			trigger = { 
				OR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = eccentric
					has_trait = impatient
				}	
			}
			animation = eyeroll
		}
		animation = personality_forgiving
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:chaplain
		animation = sadness
	}

	trigger = {	
		exists = cp:councillor_court_chaplain
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { has_trait = arrogant }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		save_scope_as = liege
		cp:councillor_court_chaplain = {
			save_scope_as = chaplain
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_lacking_intellectual_self_esteem
				years = 10
			}
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # Your humility is why you deserve the job
		name = VIETmisc.0384.a
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:chaplain = {
			remove_character_modifier = VIET_lacking_intellectual_self_esteem
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_encouraged_by_others
				years = 5
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_encouragement
			}					
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Perhaps you should just study more
		name = VIETmisc.0384.b
		stress_impact = {
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:chaplain = {
			duel = {
				skill = learning
				value = average_skill_rating
				10 = { # Failure
					compare_modifier = {
						value = scope:duel_value
						multiplier = -0.8
						min = -49
					}
					desc = VIETmisc.0384.b.toast.failure
					scope:liege = {
						send_interface_toast = {
							type = event_toast_effect_bad
							left_icon = scope:chaplain
							title = VIETmisc.0384.b.toast.failure
							scope:chaplain = {	
								stress_impact = {
									base = medium_stress_impact_gain
								}
								add_opinion = {
									target = scope:liege
									modifier = frustrated_opinion
									opinion = -15
								}
							}	
						}
					}
				}
				10 = { # Success
					compare_modifier = {
						value = scope:duel_value
						multiplier = 0.8
						min = -49
					}
					desc = VIETmisc.0384.b.toast.success
					scope:liege = {
						send_interface_toast = {
							type = event_toast_effect_good
							left_icon = scope:chaplain
							title = VIETmisc.0384.b.toast.success
							scope:chaplain = {
								add_learning_skill = 1
								stress_impact = {
									base = medium_stress_impact_loss
								}
								add_character_modifier = {
									modifier = VIET_encouraged_by_others
									years = 10
								}
								add_opinion = {
									target = root
									modifier = VIET_opinion_encouragement
								}						
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}			
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Just do your job
		name = VIETmisc.0384.c
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	

}

		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			probably_unintelligent_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			probably_intelligent_trigger = yes
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		liege = {
			save_scope_as = liege
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # Do your job
		name = VIETmisc.0387.a
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_dutiful_but_overworked
			years = 8
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Take a break
		name = VIETmisc.0387.b
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}		
	}	
}

# Silver Above Beauty (沂水秀才): Two fox spirits show a scholar silver, a calligraphy scroll, and themselves
VIETmisc.0390 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0390.t
	window = big_event_window
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						VIET_is_sinosphere_government_trigger = yes
						culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_chinese }
						knows_language = language_chinese
					}
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0390.desc.chinese
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0390.desc.non_chinese
		}
		desc = VIETmisc.0390.desc
	}
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = study }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = reading
		camera = camera_event_center_pointing_slighty_left
	}
	
	center_portrait = {
		character = scope:fox_spirit_1
		animation = fanning
		camera = camera_event_right_pointing_right_scheme
		hide_info = yes
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:fox_spirit_2
		animation = fanning_coyly
		camera = camera_event_center_pointing_very_left
		#camera = camera_event_very_right
		#camera = camera_event_far_right_very_right
		hide_info = yes
	}

	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		is_female = no
		OR = {
			has_sexuality = heterosexual
			has_sexuality = bisexual
		}
		is_playable_character = yes
		VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
		# OR = {
		# 	VIET_is_sinosphere_government_trigger = yes
		# 	government_is_japanese_trigger = yes
		# }
		NOT = { learning <= low_skill_rating }
		OR = {
			learning >= mediocre_skill_rating
			has_trait = confucian_education
			has_trait = scholar
			has_trait = lifestyle_poet
			has_trait = theologian
			has_trait = education_learning_3
			has_trait = education_learning_4
			has_trait = education_learning_5
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.3
			age >= 40
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		root.location.county = { save_scope_as = county }
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_fox_spirit_template
			faith = scope:county.faith
			culture = scope:county.culture
			save_scope_as = fox_spirit_1
		}
		create_character = {
			location = root.location
			template = VIET_fox_spirit_template
			faith = scope:county.faith
			culture = scope:county.culture
			save_scope_as = fox_spirit_2
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Take the silver
		name = VIETmisc.0390.a
		show_as_tooltip = {
			add_gold = { 5 100 }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			confucian_education = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		set_variable = {
			name = VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice
			value = flag:silver
			days = 1
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Take the scroll
		name = VIETmisc.0390.b
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice
			value = flag:scroll
			days = 1
		}	
	}	
	
	option = { # Ignore the fox spirits
		name = VIETmisc.0390.c
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
		set_variable = {
			name = VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice
			value = flag:ignore
			days = 1
		}

		# hidden_effect = {
		# 	send_interface_toast = {
		# 		left_icon = ROOT
		# 		title = VIETmisc.0390.c.toast
		# 		stress_impact = {
		# 			base = minor_stress_impact_loss
		# 		}
		# 	}			
		# }
		#scope:fox_spirit_1 ?= { silent_disappearance_effect = yes }
		#scope:fox_spirit_2 ?= { silent_disappearance_effect = yes }

	}	

	after = {
		trigger_event = VIETmisc.0391
		# if = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
		# 	}
		# 	custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0390.info
		# }
	}

}


# Silver Above Beauty (沂水秀才): the result
VIETmisc.0391 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0391.t
	window = big_event_window
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0391.desc.silver
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:scroll
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0391.desc.scroll
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:ignore
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0391.desc.ignore
			}
			# Fallback
			desc = VIETmisc.0391.desc.neutral
		}
	}
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = study }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		triggered_animation = {
			trigger = {
				var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver
				OR = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = vengeful
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
			animation = personality_vengeful
		}
		triggered_animation = {
			trigger = {
				var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver
				NOR = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = vengeful
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
			}
			animation = shame
		}
		triggered_animation = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver }
				OR = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = vengeful
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = greedy
				}
			}
			animation = paranoia
		}
		animation = personality_rational
		camera = camera_event_center_close_to_right
	}
	
	center_portrait = {
		character = scope:fox_spirit_1
		animation = fanning_coyly
		camera = camera_event_right_pointing_left_away
		hide_info = yes
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:fox_spirit_2
		animation = fanning_coyly
		camera = camera_event_right_fully_away
		#camera = camera_event_very_right
		#camera = camera_event_far_right_very_right
		hide_info = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = {
			trigger = {
				var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver
			}
			text = VIETmisc.0391.a.bad
		}
		name = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver }
			}
			text = VIETmisc.0391.a.good
		}
		flavor = VIETmisc.0391.a.flavor
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:silver
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0391.a.tooltip
			VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
				wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
				generous = minor_stress_impact_gain
				arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:scroll
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_loss
				confucian_education = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				scholar = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				education_learning_3 = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				education_learning_4 = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				education_learning_5 = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice ?= flag:ignore
			}
			add_learning_lifestyle_xp = minor_lifestyle_xp
			if = {
				limit = { has_trait = confucian_education }
				add_trait_xp = {
					trait = confucian_education
					value = lifestyle_confucian_education_xp_gain_minor_value
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				calm = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
		}

	}	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice }
			remove_variable = VIET_silver_over_beauty_choice
		}
		scope:fox_spirit_1 ?= { silent_disappearance_effect = yes }
		scope:fox_spirit_2 ?= { silent_disappearance_effect = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0391.info
		}
	}

}



# Monk of Changqing (长清僧): Old monk dies, and his ghost accidentally possesses a young man who just died
VIETmisc.0392 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0392.t
	window = big_event_window
	desc = VIETmisc.0392.desc
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { reference = study }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:monk
		animation = prayer
		camera = camera_event_group_talking_left_left
	}

	lower_center_portrait = scope:manager

	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		is_playable_character = yes
		OR = {
			VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			age <= 40
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
			has_no_particular_noble_roots_trigger = yes
			NOT = { is_close_family_of = root }
			is_clergy = no
			NOT = { has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain }
			NOT = { has_trait = devoted }
		}
		capital_county.duchy.kingdom = {
			any_in_de_jure_hierarchy = {
				tier = tier_county
				NOT = { holder = root }
				holder = { is_ai = yes }
				OR = {
					holder.faith = { has_doctrine = special_doctrine_immaterial_harmony }
					holder.religion = religion:buddhism_religion	
				}		
				any_county_province = {
					has_holding_type = church_holding
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		capital_county.duchy.kingdom = {
			random_in_de_jure_hierarchy = {
				limit = {
					tier = tier_county
					NOT = { holder = root }
					holder = { is_ai = yes }
					OR = {
						holder.faith = { has_doctrine = special_doctrine_immaterial_harmony }
						holder.religion = religion:buddhism_religion	
					}		
					any_county_province = {
						has_holding_type = church_holding
					}					
				}
				holder = {
					save_scope_as = manager
				}
				random_county_province = {
					limit = {
						has_holding_type = church_holding
					}
					save_scope_as = location
				}
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				age <= 40
				religion = religion:buddhism_religion
				has_no_particular_noble_roots_trigger = yes
				NOT = { is_close_family_of = root }
				is_clergy = no
				NOT = { has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain }
				NOT = { has_trait = devoted }
			}		
			save_scope_as = monk
		}
		scope:monk = {
			VIET_remove_personality_traits_effect = yes	
			add_trait = calm
			add_trait = humble
			add_trait = temperate
			add_trait = devoted			
			add_trait = celibate			
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_possessed_by_a_dead_monk
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0392.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					faith = { has_doctrine = special_doctrine_immaterial_harmony }
					religion = religion:buddhism_religion	
				}		
			}
			VIET_massive_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_massive_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		}
		scope:manager = {
			add_courtier = scope:monk
		}
		scope:monk = {			
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = pleased_opinion
				target = root
				opinion = 10
			}
			add_character_flag = {
				flag = blocked_from_leaving
				years = 50
			}				
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Try to get them back
		name = VIETmisc.0392.b
		VIET_massive_piety_loss_effect = yes
		duel = {
			skill = intrigue
			target = scope:monk
			10 = { # Failure
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = -1.1
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0392.b.toast_bad
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = scope:monk
					title = VIETmisc.0392.b.toast_bad
					scope:manager = {
						add_courtier = scope:monk
					}
					scope:monk = {
						add_character_flag = {
							flag = blocked_from_leaving
							years = 50
						}				
						add_opinion = {
							modifier = disappointed_opinion
							target = root
							opinion = -10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			10 = { # Success
				compare_modifier = {
					value = scope:duel_value
					multiplier = 1.1
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0392.b.toast_good
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = scope:monk
					title = VIETmisc.0392.b.toast_good
					scope:monk = {
						add_opinion = {
							modifier = disappointed_opinion
							target = root
							opinion = -50
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			generous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0392.info
		}
	}

}


# Dragon Dormant (蛰龙): Encounter a mysterious dragon from a book - a Qing Dynasty depiction of this story is the picture of cybrxkhan's profile in some places!
VIETmisc.0393 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0393.t
	window = big_event_window
	desc = VIETmisc.0393.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { reference = study }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = storyteller
	}

	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		is_playable_character = yes
		VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
			}		
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0393.a
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0393.b
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}	

	after = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_dragon_dormant
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = amused_opinion
				opinion = 5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0393.info
		}
	}

}


# Sheep Skin (某公): Person recalls their reincarnation where they were initially condemned to be reborn as a sheep
VIETmisc.0394 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0394.t
	window = big_event_window
	desc = VIETmisc.0394.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { reference = relaxing_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = pondering
		camera = camera_event_scheme_center_look_right
	}
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = storyteller
	}

	trigger = {	
		has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events
		is_playable_character = yes
		OR = {
			VIET_is_sinosphere_trigger = yes
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			religion = religion:buddhism_religion
			dynasty != root.dynasty
			NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}	

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				religion = religion:buddhism_religion
				dynasty != root.dynasty
				NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
			}		
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
		scope:courtier = {			
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_sheepskin_rebirth
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0394.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			arbitrary = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			eccentric = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0394.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		
	}	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0394.info
		}
	}

}
